Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee  

Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
Standstill and Advancement  
<Prayer> Father, as we look back on the path of restoration you have left behind, may we remember the weak children who, in this battlefield where they determine their current position, realize their own inadequacy and, looking up to heaven alone, long for your holy touch.  
Father, how many of our ancestors have looked up to heaven and pleaded with you, the source of power, to save them? As we recall the images of these ancestors, may we take this time to reflect on our own humble state today and realize once again that we are not yet in a position to sincerely call you Father.  
We must recognize that we need to serve heaven with all our heart, acknowledge you as our Father, and firmly understand that we are your children placed before you. When we think about whether we can truly call you Father and whether you can call us your children, we realize how inadequate we are and that we cannot even establish the face to call you Father.  
Father, you have gathered us this morning, so please look upon each individual. When we realize that the issue has been our yearning for goodness and our admiration for you, we, the inadequate ones, cannot help but seek your forgiveness once again.  
June 14, 1970 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
8   Standstill and Advancement  
We must realize how unfortunate and sorrowful it is to be the fallen descendants who must always live on the path of sorrow, and we must lament that we cannot even entertain such thoughts. We must understand that when we fail to stand in such a position, you, Father, must stand in that position once again. If I do not feel sorrow, you will feel sorrow; if I do not grieve, you will grieve; if I do not strive, you must strive; and if I do not fight, you must fight.  
I must understand that you and I are not in corresponding positions but rather in opposing positions, where I can be in a place of joy while you are in a place of sorrow, and when I am in a place of sorrow, you can be in a place of joy. As I reflect on this paradoxical path of destiny, may I become your sons and daughters who can critique my tomorrow. Father, I earnestly wish and desire this.  
Father, are there your sons and daughters across the nation who are looking up to heaven with tears this morning? Your mercy will dwell in that place, goodness will begin from there, and the connection of your heart will sprout from that place. Therefore, we must firmly understand that fallen humanity must walk the path of tears. The path we have walked, fighting against sorrow, loneliness, and pain, is the path that countless saints have walked toward heaven, and it is the historical path left by good ancestors. We must realize that we must devote ourselves to such a path and that the path of life awaits us, which we must walk through every single day from this moment onward.  
Thus, we must recognize that our journey is bound by historical sin, which prevents us from rejoicing. We must understand that all the conditions of the times are restraining me and blocking tomorrow's liberation. Therefore, I earnestly ask and wish for these individuals to realize that all efforts are necessary to break through and overcome these conditions.  
9  
Before the foundation of your calling, before the path of sorrow you have walked, we must discover our true selves, who must become true filial sons and daughters who can comfort you, Father. We must also discover our true selves, who must become loyal subjects of the nation you desire. Without this, we cannot draw near to you, Father, so I earnestly wish and desire that we can once again realize and keep this in mind.  
How lonely it must be for your children scattered around the world to long for this land of Korea and to devote their hearts toward it! I earnestly hope and wish that you will remember those poor souls. If there are children shedding tears while longing for this place, I believe you will sympathize with them, comparing their situation with the tears you have shed while seeking humanity. Please look upon the stories of our lives as we hope to spend such days, Father, with compassion.  
If you were not here, we know that living in such a position and continuing such a life before heaven, before humanity, and before the historical era would be meaningless. In this place where such a life continues, Father, please come and be with us and bless us. I earnestly wish and desire this.  
Father, although we are far apart from your children scattered around the world in the physical realm, may we realize how precious it is that we move together in the realm of the heart centered on one point. Through such a connection, may we be victorious today and victorious tomorrow, and throughout our lives, Father, protect us and hold us tightly so that you do not let go.  
We know that the world they desire is the world we desire, so please allow us to feel every sensation and emotion we experience in our daily lives together with our companions. We have also learned that when the emotional stories we share with them align with your story, true brotherhood is established. When the connection between Cain and Abel is established from one end of the earth to the other, we understand that the foundation for restoration will be established.  
10   Standstill and Advancement  
Thus, many people have cried out for the heart of compassion on behalf of humanity throughout the historical process, advocating not only for their own nation but also for the love of all humanity. However, there has been no group that has truly lived in love and harmony with the Father in such a position. We are grateful for your grace that has allowed us to establish such a connection today, knowing the sorrow of the historical era.  
Their sorrow is our sorrow, and their wishes are our wishes. We earnestly hope and wish that they may realize how valuable it is that all their desires align with your will. Their sorrow does not end as their own sorrow alone. The sorrow of the East connects with the West, and the sorrow of the West connects with the East, and the sorrow of the earth must connect with the sorrow of heaven. We also understand that we cannot advance even one step without resolving the greater sorrow of the Father than our own. Father, who looks upon the stories of humanity that must shed such tears, may we realize once again this morning that you have also shed tears alongside such stories.  
Among your children who bow their heads, if there are sons and daughters who can align with your heart and your feelings, whether they are men or women, we must understand that the point of emotional connection between them becomes the foundation where you can work. When viewed on an individual level, we know that the body and mind must find a point of unity. By establishing such points of connection where we can give and receive, we must realize that without establishing points of unity from individuals to families, tribes, nations, and all men and women of the world, and even the entire realm of heaven and earth, we cannot have a connection of life.  
We understand that connections made solely among humans will end with humanity itself and cannot connect to eternal life. Knowing this, we do not wish for a beginning, connection, and end that is solely human. We earnestly ask and wish that you may be the center, allowing us to fulfill the starting point, process, purpose, and results.  
Father, how much do our hearts long for you? How earnestly have our bodies bowed before you? How deeply are our bodies and minds filled with the desire to call upon you? How fervently do we wish to dedicate our entire being before you?  
If there are any shortcomings in this regard, please forgive us, and may you make their hearts earnest, enabling them to strive to become one. We earnestly wish and desire that if such connections do not manifest here, they can only lead to a foundation of death. Knowing this, Father, who watches over us, do not leave us in the world of death but come and find us. We earnestly wish and desire this.  
Father, we must become beings who can be absorbed into your realm of life. To do so, we must disappear. May we enter into a state of complete nothingness, allowing only the thought of your desired will to arise from our hearts and be absorbed into your movements. We earnestly wish and desire this, Father.  
If you have sons and daughters you wish to send forth, please send them. Let your will be fulfilled. We know that your desired will must be realized, so we wish to advance toward the day when your will is fulfilled. Father, please guide us and support us to overcome the abyss of resentment caused by the fall.  
Today is the Sabbath, so please preside over this day and manage everything so that we may reach a place of good results. Please look upon the children who have gathered. May our bodies and minds become one, and may this entire audience unite in the holy connection that allows us to align with all your desires. I earnestly request this, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.  
12   Standstill and Advancement  
<Words> In our lives, standstill and advancement serve as the motives that determine success or failure. We often see how these factors influence whether things prosper or perish in our daily surroundings.  
The Ultimate Boundary of Advancement Desired by God and Humanity  
Everyone wishes to prosper. No one desires to perish. Everyone wants to develop and be revealed in their environment. This applies not only to individuals but also to families. Because families are like this, nations formed by their connection also hope for the same. If nations desire this, it goes without saying that the world does too. Since we humans are like this, it is likely that God, who created humanity, desires the same.  
In guiding human history, God does not wish for the reality of that history to come to a standstill. We must understand that God desires advancement and development beyond stagnation.  
So, what will be the ultimate boundary of advancement, the highest limit to which we can move forward? It must not be a place where God and humanity are separated. The highest boundary of advancement must be a place where God and we can unite more strongly and become one more powerfully. That place is undoubtedly a world of oneness.  
So, what must be centered to create a world of oneness? It goes without saying that we must unite centered on God's love. No matter how good something is in this world, it is worthless unless it establishes a relationship with oneself. No matter how precious something is, it is useless. It must establish a relationship with oneself to shine. Furthermore, even if that precious thing has established a relationship with oneself, that relationship must not be temporary but eternal. No matter how valuable an existence may be, if it lacks eternal content, it cannot avoid falling into a worthless state. Even if something precious has united with me, if it does not contain eternity, it is of no use. Only by transcending the limits of time and centering on eternity can we find a love that can be loved more and a higher connection of love, and only then can we truly become a connection of infinite value.  
In the world, people often regard their beloved children as the most precious standard. When we consider love, what is the limit of a parent's love for their child? Parents do not only want to love their children when they are young; they wish to love them throughout their lives and even into eternity. If a relationship of parent and child can be established through love, where both feel fulfillment and value, then infinite strength, infinite stimulation, and infinitely new experiences arise within that relationship. A relationship that lacks such connections will inevitably be interrupted at some point.  
When a relationship that was connected as true, the best, and of infinite value is interrupted, unless something greater can replace it to support that value, that value becomes a condition of sorrow.
Therefore, when we possess or embrace something of precious value, the question arises as to how we can develop it into something of even greater value. Precious and infinite value cannot be obtained through any material or external connections in the human world. It must be through the connection of love that holds a more precious content. This connection of love must not be established through a third party but should be formed through a direct relationship to truly feel the infinite value.

What is the ultimate boundary of progress that God and humanity desire? As mentioned, it is the place where we unite centered on love. This unification does not end at any specific point, boundary, or time frame; rather, it must transcend time and continue to develop further. Without such factors, love cannot provide infinite happiness. If one claims happiness without reaching such a boundary, it can only be considered happiness below that boundary. The ultimate point that God wishes to find with humanity is to surpass a point that can infinitely stimulate love centered on infinite love. This standard must become the highest criterion for progress.

When we examine ourselves based on this standard, the question is whether we have become capable of doing so. Even if we have not yet become capable, we must strive to become so. If we are not even making efforts to become capable, we must at least prepare to do so. If we do not even have the desire to strive for that, we must understand that we will inevitably face the issue of stagnation.

It is essential for love to involve the connection of life. 

While taking a brief break from work is acceptable, if one simply stagnates without preparing to move forward or making any effort while there is still a path ahead, that person will come to an end there. No matter how capable one may be, in a stagnant position, one cannot establish relationships with all beings or the world of existence, as those existences will not seek to form relationships. We can observe this fact in our daily lives.

When you seek to make friends, the question becomes whether they are friends who can develop or friends who hold no hope. The more you establish relationships with friends who hold no hope, the more worthless results will inevitably manifest in your life. Therefore, it is essential to form relationships with better friends and prepare and strive for a better tomorrow.

So, what will you use to make such efforts? You must strive with a loving heart. Thus, the question becomes how much of that loving heart is invested.

Love cannot be achieved alone. Without the input of life, love cannot be established. Even in the love of a wealthy relationship, there is a connection of life involved. As long as there remains a connection of life, as long as there is a desire within that connection of life, there will inevitably be a connection of love. You cannot establish a relationship of love apart from the connection of life.

Therefore, love must necessarily involve the connection of life. Furthermore, the extent to which life is invested in love determines whether it is felt as more valuable or not.

For example, a parent's love for a child is not merely through a mundane relationship; it is a love that emanates from the very bones and marrow. Parents possess a love that cannot be forgotten or severed. As long as there is life left in them, parents will love their children. When they feel the connection of life with their children, the love for their children naturally arises from within them. It is not a conscious decision to love because the child is their son; rather, it is because their life force is inherently connected to the child that they cannot help but love.

The same applies to the love between spouses. To say, "I love you because we have a connection," is not love. Love between a wife and a husband must involve the investment of their lives, and the life force that can transcend oneself must be exchanged to stimulate love between them; only then can the love between spouses endure eternally.

Loving a nation is also the same. The phrase "I love my country," or "I am a patriot," necessarily involves a connection of life. A true patriot is determined only after transcending life. Within the precious internal connections of loyalty, filial piety, or love, life is always intertwined. Moreover, the degree to which these connections are tied to life determines whether they are valuable or worthless, or whether they are eternal or temporary.

From this perspective, God's love for humanity is also the same. The infinite love of God, or the infinite life of God, determines whether I possess infinite value based on how much it affects me. We must understand this.

Today, as we strive to progress, the same applies. Love without life is confined within a limited time frame. We do not need love that is confined within a time frame. That is, love that is limited to a certain time, such as "I will love only until my parents are alive" or "I will love only while I am alive," is not true love. Love must be pursued naturally through one's life force, not with the intention of deliberately crossing boundaries. Love must occur in a place where life connections are already established beyond one's consciousness, and only then can eternal connections be formed.

The issues that religious people have sought to resolve

When we say that God loves the world, it does not mean that He loves a specific individual only during their lifetime, whether it be 70 years or 80 years. God loves that individual through countless ancestors and through the current humanity. He loves their descendants eternally. This is why God's love is necessary. Moreover, that love does not end with itself; it is connected to life, which is why God's love is essential.

Wherever God's love encounters challenges, God's life is always present. Because of the position that accompanies life, the love of heaven can be connected, allowing both God and oneself to find joy together.

In friendships, the depth of friendship can be determined by how much of life can be shared within that friendship.

From this perspective, the standard for progress can be said to be the highest position where life and love are intertwined. Without such a position, one cannot hope for the purpose or value of progress.

Today, if humanity has the desire to develop or progress, where will that boundary of hope lie? It lies in the place where the world unites centered around me, rather than just uniting with a particular nation. Furthermore, it does not end with the world uniting around me; it is the place where God's love and the connection of God's life are linked with the world through me. When humanity stands in such a position, we can finally say that progress has reached its boundary.

When we reach such a standard, my joy does not end with my own joy. It does not end with God's joy either. When God and I rejoice, everything within this environment will inevitably be filled with joy.

When you consider yourself, when you say you are joyful, that joy is not only felt in your heart but is felt throughout your entire body and mind. Similarly, when the connection of love is established between God and humanity, the love and life of God collide, allowing us to feel love of infinite value. This love does not end with just God and humanity; it can become the life force and love of the entire existence, and we must understand this fact.

When such connections are formed, the life connections of the whole will be activated. Even if that connection is a linear exchange between subject and object, it will involve both flat and three-dimensional content, and the entire environment will be resurrected within the realm of love and life.

From this perspective, that realm can be a state where cosmic life and cosmic love overflow, allowing us to experience infinite value. It can be said to be the highest position where there is no greater value. It is the boundary of the greatest hope and a place where infinite value can be felt. We must recognize that such a place is the most precious place for humanity.

Then, how do we seek out such a place? This was the problem that countless religious figures and those on the path of virtue have sought to resolve. Have they not worked hard to solve such problems? In light of this boundary, we must once again clarify what position we are in today.

Have you ever had a heart that loves humanity? If you do not have a heart that loves humanity, do you have a heart that loves your nation? If you do not have a heart that loves your nation, do you have a heart that loves your tribe or relatives? If you do not have a heart that loves your relatives, do you have a heart that loves your siblings? If so, within that love, you must feel that your own life is invested, that your own flesh and blood are involved. When love is severed, you should feel pain. You should feel sorrow. The magnitude of sorrow is determined by the extent of the emotional depletion from oneself. If you separate those who love each other, what would be the reason to restore that connection, even at the cost of life? It is because love exists in a place that transcends life.

What position are we in today?

So, do you have a heart of love that transcends the connection of life within your living realm centered on yourself, or are you moving toward the hopeful world of tomorrow, the world of God's love tomorrow? Are you in a position of progress or stagnation?

You may often experience this even within your habitual living realm. However, we know that many people live without any stimulation, unaware of whether such things exist or not. A person who wakes up in the morning, washes their face, eats breakfast, and goes to work, living such a habitual life is a worthless person. 

Such a person cannot become a patriot who loves their country. We must understand that their lives are lived without even loving themselves. In daily life and social interactions, the extent to which one invests their love and life into relationships within their workplace or organization determines whether they lead a fulfilling social life or an unfulfilling one.

From this perspective, the question is what position our individual selves are in. Especially for those in a position of faith, this can become an even greater issue. Pursuing the world of eternal life is the essence of faith. Pursuing the eternal love of God is faith. To align with eternal life and eternal love, finding the point where God's joy and my joy meet to feel not two joys but one joy is the path of faith. Therefore, it is of utmost importance to consider how much progressive love and life force we possess as individuals engaged in faith.

The value of a human being is determined by how much we relate to life or love through the integration of all the sensations we perceive through our senses. Thus, we cannot help but reconsider whether we have formed relationships and lived socially with a heart filled with life force and weighted love. If we are not standing in such a position, we must understand that we are either stagnating or retreating.

No one welcomes retreat. Those who retreat are not befriended or sought after by anyone. Only those in a position of progress seek to unite and become friends. So, are we stagnating today? Are we progressing? Or are we retreating? Above all, this is the question we must contemplate.

Today, in our lives of faith, the question arises whether our lives since the day we resolved to pursue our purpose have been in a position of stagnation, progress, or retreat. Some may have lived for a year, some for ten years, or even half their lives with purpose, but the question remains whether that life has been stagnant, progressing, or retreating. You must clearly identify where you fall within this spectrum. No matter how much you may have progressed in the past, if you are stagnant today, there can be no life force of God present. There can be no connection of God's love. Even if you lived in the past with infinite value, infinite life force, and infinite love, if you are in a stagnant position now, you must understand that you are separated from God.

So, what position are you in? Are you stagnant, progressing, or retreating? You must recognize that the scales of fate weigh heavily on you, whether you are progressing today or whether you are stagnant or retreating after having progressed in the past.

Stagnation is close to retreat, while progress is close to the destination. A stagnant position is near the line of death, while overcoming stagnation and progressing brings one closer to the line of life. Our life journey is to walk along these two boundaries, leading life forward.

The eternal progress of God's love

So, what about God's love? Is the infinite love of God stagnant in the history of the ages? Is it progressing? Or is it retreating? If God's love is infinite and God's life is infinite, then until we reach that point, that life and love cannot be stagnant. If that love and life cannot be stagnant, if they possess the power to infinitely extend and progress, then God's providence must only experience development. However, if that love and life force is halted, God's providence of salvation must inevitably fall below the boundary.
The leaders know. Therefore, we can conclude that there cannot be a halt in the world of God's love. Thus, the statement that God's life force is halted must be denied. Since the life force of God has never been halted from the day humanity fell until now, it follows that there has never been a time when God's love was halted.

In the face of the hope of such history and the love and life of God that have continued without interruption until now, if our individual selves are halted today, we must recognize that there is no greater rebellion against God than this. For thousands of years, God's providential hand has tirelessly sought to establish us in our own selves and to lead us to the limits of the world of purpose. If I forget that hand, deny it, and come to a halt, I become an unacceptable being before God. If it is disobedience, there can be no greater disobedience; if it is unfaithfulness, there can be no greater unfaithfulness; if it is evil, there can be no greater evil. We must understand this. If someone thinks, "Why is it that God's life force and love do not come to a halt, yet I am always inclined to halt?" then they must engage in a profound repentance.

In living a life of faith, do you have the explosive and stimulating power within your heart to constantly move toward the world of purpose? If you have such a heart, it is evidence that God is with you. Conversely, if you lack such power, it is evidence that God is separated from you.

If the heart that loves humanity rises within you and the desire to share your life with humanity does not cease, it is a testimony that you belong to heaven. However, if that love is centered on oneself and ends with boasting of one's own value, it is evidence that God has already separated from you. The path of such a person is not toward heaven. Such a person will reach a limit centered on themselves. The world centered on oneself is different from the world of God's will.

You must critically assess whether you are someone who can go to heaven, or whether you must go to hell, or whether you should remain in the intermediate spiritual realm. This can be clearly understood from the perspective of halt and advance. If your heart is filled with life force and a love that forgets your own self and loves your nation and humanity, you are undoubtedly a heavenly people heading toward heaven, and you are undoubtedly a heavenly people heading toward the world.

However, if you forget your nation and purpose and center everything around yourself, you will be in a state of halt. Therefore, heaven will depart from you. The heaven that is centered on oneself is unnecessary. You must enter and live in the heaven that is within the realm of God's love and God's life. That heaven is, after all, a heaven that transcends the world. Those who seek a heaven centered on themselves claim a heaven within their self-centered realm. According to such claims, God must enter and live within that realm. Therefore, such a heaven cannot exist.

Faith cannot be practiced without repentance.

We are looking forward to a greater world where such a love can dwell. A heaven centered on a person who is unable to solve their own frustrating problems and is in a state of halt cannot exist. Those who belong to a lower position are undeniably beings belonging to hell. Therefore, you must understand that the word "halt" is an extremely fearful word.

When you began your church life, that is, when you set out on this path according to the will, you came forth with the holy title of national restoration. When that national restoration reaches its limit, you can hope for the day when you can raise the new banner of world restoration, overcoming all adversities and environments. Such a person, who has the ability to do so, is heading straight for heaven. Conversely, a person who is in a state of halt or retreat, that is, someone who turns back from their forward steps within the national heavenly realm and heads toward their individual desires, is undoubtedly heading toward hell.

In today's living environment, if a leader gives a command or instruction for the sake of the will and you do not have the strength to say, "Let's go!" it proves that you are already in a state of halt. Even when a command for a full advance toward the goal has been given, if you are indifferent to that command and your life's inspiration is not connected to it, then you are already in a state of halt.

Let us think about what to do with those who are in such a state of halt. No matter how much you advise or stimulate them, if they say it has nothing to do with them, they have fallen into a position where they cannot rise again. To raise such people again, a tremendous effort must be made. Even if you give them a certain amount of strength, if they remain indifferent, you cannot move them without increasing that strength significantly.

So how can we help such people move again? You must understand that without causing them loss centered on God, they cannot rise again. Such a person must feel that they have caused loss before God and must pay the price for that loss. That position must be one where they feel infinite sorrow. However, if a person in such a position forgets even the feeling of sorrow, they will be someone without hope forever.

In the depths of your hearts, the question is whether you have the desire to go along with the will, or with the world, or with heaven based on this standard. Those who go to church out of obligation due to connections with friends, or who cannot resist the encouragement of friends and follow the path of the will, are proving that they do not possess life force.

So, are you advancing now? Are you at a halt? Are you retreating? This is the issue you must resolve from now on. If there are those who are advancing, do not slow down your pace of advance. If the heart that loves individuals is burning, it must not end only with that individual. You must think about how to connect that heart to the nation and to the world. If the love for individuals does not connect to the love for the world, you must find a way to connect it. Furthermore, the question is how to connect that heart to God's love and God's life.

For fallen beings like us to enter into the realm of God's life and love, repentance is absolutely necessary. If we have committed the sins of a hundred sheep from our ancestors until now, we must make even greater efforts and repent. That is why repentance cannot be omitted in the life of faith. We were born through countless ancestors. If those ancestors were good, I am automatically in close proximity to God's life realm. However, if the ancestors were evil, I am far from God's life realm. For someone far away to connect with God's life realm, a period of repentance that surpasses all the evils committed by the ancestors is absolutely necessary. Without fulfilling this, one cannot connect with a world of life force beyond oneself. Therefore, you must understand that tears of repentance are essential on the path of faith.

The greatest gift of love that God has given to humanity.

If you cannot repent and advance on your own, you must have companions in faith. You need someone who can hold you up. If the place you must go is a heaven that transcends the world, then you must love that person, mustn't you? This is a reasonable demand.

If you have a good friend among those you love, you must hold on to them tightly. By respecting them more than your own life and having an absolute heart of obedience to their words, if you strive to follow their guidance, you can escape your current position through them. If that person is in a position of a million, you can also reach that position of a million. Therefore, if there is someone in a position of ten million, everyone wants to unite with that person. That is why we seek better friends and better teachers.

God knows that humans need companions, which is why He cannot help but send the most precious Messiah. Because God loves humanity, He must send a representative being who can connect with humanity, someone like a friend, a teacher, and even a father. This representative being is the Messiah.

You must understand that the Messiah is our unparalleled friend, unparalleled teacher, and unparalleled father. The one sent to this earth as the greatest being, the one and only, is the Messiah. Therefore, if you hold on to that Messiah, shed tears for Him, invest your life for Him, and love Him as your own life, you can enter into the realm of God's life and love, which is historical and cosmic. This is the greatest gift of love that God has given to humanity.

That is why countless saints who have centered their faith on Christianity and believed in Jesus have invested their lives for Him. They did not only invest their lives; they invested all their love as well. Those who died did not die along with death but resurrected along with Jesus' love and Jesus' life. This is the gift of resurrection through Christianity, which God loves.

You must be able to invest your life for the Messiah. Such a person is wise. If someone can invest not only their life but also all their love, they are exceedingly wise.

Why? Humanity has pursued the path of advancement to become a subject being capable of loving the world or loving heaven and earth. Becoming such a being is the purpose for which humanity has pursued the path of advancement. The only way to achieve that purpose all at once or in one generation is to receive the Messiah and leave behind the connection of having invested your life and love. Then, it does not end there. Because you have given everything, you will stand in a position to receive everything. Thus, you will be granted the privilege to reach the glory of Christ and the realm of Christ's life and love without shame.

What path must fallen humanity take today? It is the path of repentance. Therefore, we must seek the path of repentance. There can be no love for the nation from one who does not repent, and there can be no love for the world from one who does not repent.

So where do we find the connection to repent? We find it through people. In seeking it through people, we need the Messiah. He appears as the friend of friends, the teacher of teachers, and the parent of parents. To love Him completely is to enter the realm where we can love the world He loves and the heaven and earth He must love. We must remember that without establishing a connection with Him, we cannot love.

That is why God has sent numerous religious leaders to this earth to seek this path. Among those religious leaders, the one who comes in the name of the Father, in the name of the greatest teacher, and in the name of the greatest friend is the Messiah. Meeting that Messiah is the greatest happiness for fallen humanity, and the place where one meets Him is the place of the highest glory.

Thus, the history of humanity has sought that place. Before seeking the world, we must welcome Him. If a family welcomes Him and lives with Him, that family can become a realm of heaven. If a nation welcomes Him and fulfills the duty of loyalty centered on Him, through that connection of loyalty, they can find the nation. When we fulfill the duties of filial piety and loyalty before God centered on Him, we must understand that the world will be found.

If such a being exists, the question is how well do you know Him, and how much will you accept and follow His commands? If He gives a command of a million in value, it is not a command given from a position of a hundred. You must understand that He commands from a position of ten million in value. And that command contains a heart of love and life force. However, if you cannot move according to that command and cannot advance with it, you must understand that the conditions for unimaginable misfortune will block your path.

If a command is given and you cannot practice it, that failure to practice will block all paths that are related to Him and that you must walk. Therefore, even if He commanded with a value of a million, because He commanded with a value of ten million, if you disbelieve and disobey that command, you will incur great loss. To make up for this loss, you must repent infinitely for not keeping that command. Otherwise, you cannot walk a greater path. This is a just principle.

You who have entered the path of the will, how did you become exhausted and find yourselves on the path of retreat below the state of halt? What is the cause? When the teacher gives a command of a million in value, it is not given with a value of a million but with a higher, more sophisticated value of ten million. If you betray that, the greater grace will be blocked. And you must understand that the infinite life force of God cannot leave.

Realizing that you are in such a position, what should you do? You must go to a position beyond what you have lost. However, the question is how to go out from that position. When God commanded from a position of a million and I could not practice it, what should I do? You must seek a place where God can command from a position above a million. Then, you must repent of the past and aspire to a position above a hundred, pouring out all your life and all the love you have. Only then will there be a way to advance again into the eternal world of God's life and love.

Think back to the past when you entered the path of the will. When you first understood the will, you followed it not knowing if you would live or die. At that time, you went before the command was given, and when told to go to a place where you must give your life, you went with a heart willing to invest your life. At that time, because you loved and admired the will more than your own life, God was with you. More than your life, you loved the will...
지하느냐, 후퇴하느냐? 세계가 발전하느냐, 정지하느냐, 후퇴하느냐? 이러한 모든 문제는 결국 여러분이 어떻게 하느냐에 달려 있습니다. 여러분이 정지해 있거나 후퇴하고 있다면, 그것은 여러분이 하나님과의 관계에서 멀어지고 있다는 것을 의미합니다. 여러분이 전진하고 있다면, 그것은 하나님과의 관계가 깊어지고 있다는 증거입니다.

하나님은 여러분이 어떤 위치에 있든지 간에, 여러분이 그분의 뜻을 따르기를 원하십니다. 여러분이 하나님을 중심삼고 출발하여 그분의 뜻을 이루기 위해 노력한다면, 하나님은 여러분에게 힘을 주시고, 여러분의 삶을 인도하실 것입니다. 그러나 여러분이 자신을 중심삼고 살아간다면, 결국에는 그 길이 파멸로 이어질 것입니다.

여러분은 지금 어떤 선택을 하고 있습니까? 여러분의 삶에서 하나님을 중심으로 삼고 있습니까, 아니면 자신을 중심으로 삼고 있습니까? 여러분이 하나님을 중심으로 삼고 있다면, 여러분은 반드시 그분의 뜻을 이루기 위해 노력해야 합니다. 그리고 그 과정에서 여러분은 하나님과의 관계를 더욱 깊게 만들어 가야 합니다.

이제 여러분은 자신이 어떤 위치에 있는지를 분명히 알고, 그에 따라 행동해야 합니다. 여러분이 정지해 있다면, 그것을 깨닫고 회개해야 합니다. 여러분이 후퇴하고 있다면, 그것을 인식하고 다시 전진할 수 있는 길을 찾아야 합니다. 여러분이 전진하고 있다면, 그 길을 더욱 확고히 하고, 하나님과의 관계를 더욱 깊게 만들어 가야 합니다.

하나님은 여러분이 그분의 뜻을 이루기 위해 노력하는 것을 바라십니다. 여러분이 그 뜻을 이루기 위해 힘쓰고, 하나님과의 관계를 더욱 깊게 만들어 간다면, 여러분의 삶은 더욱 풍성해질 것입니다. 하나님은 여러분을 사랑하시고, 여러분이 그분의 뜻을 이루기 위해 노력하는 것을 기뻐하십니다. 그러므로 여러분은 언제나 하나님을 중심삼고 살아가야 합니다.
Will we retreat or advance? Will the Communist Party develop, stagnate, or retreat? All of this can be judged through this principle of remission. Then why is America retreating? Human Nature
