What is the difference between the 1960s and the 1970s? At the turning point of crossing a boundary, centered around May and June, we must feel that we have reached a point where we can sense the era of purpose and the heart of the Father. The more we are in such times, the more we must realize that it is a once-in-a-lifetime era where we can pledge our responsibilities and missions, and we earnestly hope that we can put forth all our hearts.

When we cannot do so, we must feel sorry day and night for not being able to offer our bodies and minds, and may we come to realize that the Father is the one who is being pursued and chased through all the processes of suffering and restoration. Before us, you are a kind Father, but behind us, you are a strict Father, and I have come to know this while following the path of suffering.

When the Father we have followed and served becomes distant, it is easy to fall into despair, and I know that the enemy appears in place of the Father. When we come to understand that the restoration providence leads us to the point where the enemy commands us to die instead of the Father, we realize that the path of indemnity in the restoration providence is not only a joyful and glorious path but also a path of sorrow that must be crossed many times. We must understand that peace does not continue in a family that knows the purpose, as it is not yet the time centered on that family. We must realize that the time when unavoidable hardships come to that family is the time when God can love it as a fruit.

Just as all the leaves fall in autumn, leaving only bare branches, the time when the true wife, true son, or true husband can reveal themselves is not a time of ease but a time of hardship. Therefore, we must be able to serve centered on the relationships that are in hardship. Only families that can seek such environments can remain forever in the heavenly and earthly realms and become your bloodline.

Father, I understand that in order for the Unification Church, which has walked until now, to remain a global church, it must go through a process where the voice of the church's conscience breaks through the barriers of darkness. I know that such a destiny is the destiny of our Unification Church today, and furthermore, it is the destiny of Korea and the destiny of Asia. I have come to understand that the breakthrough to overcome this bleak destiny can only begin through the Father, and therefore, we cannot help but put forth our hearts.

We must dedicate ourselves to saving this nation, and centered on the three thousand ri peninsula, we must put forth our hearts, so we do not want to dedicate ourselves in the name of the Unification Church. We want to dedicate ourselves in the name of the Han people and want to dedicate ourselves in honor of the loyal subjects who have come and gone in this country, so we earnestly hope that you will accept this.

Until now, we have not pledged the victory of the Unification Church. Our wish has been for the victory of this nation, and not only for the nation but also for the victory of the world. Because this is the Father’s wish, we must practice the duty of being the Father’s sons. Those who fight and wish to die along with that wish are the people of unification, so please guide them so that their path is not miserable.

We must take on the mission of pioneers and vanguards in constructing the garden of restoration where all people can live. What we do must be worthy of honor, so our appearance must never become miserable. Knowing that if there is night, there will be day, and if there is day, there will be night, even if we are currently in a dark night, we must navigate the dark path with the hope of a future day. We must overcome until the new morning comes and the morning sun rises in the east.

Father, even if we have crossed a hill that can be overcome in the 1970s, we must understand that there is still a way to go toward the bright new morning of the nation and the world. In the past, we wore old clothes and rags, but now we are at a point where we must dress formally and respectfully to solemnly accompany the Father, so we must feel even more ashamed to stand before you.

As unworthy children who cannot hide our shame, we must feel deeply ashamed before the Father, but we must go out with the heart that only wishes to serve the suffering Father. When the time comes to welcome the bright new morning in your glorious presence and to praise the heavenly connections, it is our earnest wish to stand before you as the shield of your nation and to receive that glory.

Until that day comes, may you be behind us, adjusting the providence, and we must become the appearance that can rejoice with your glory. When we meet the Father in glory on the path of restoration, we must receive the gracious blessing that says, “This victory is for you,” and we understand that the holy purpose of indemnity and restoration will be fulfilled in this world. Before such solemn circumstances, we have been too petty and too lowly. We have been too lacking in talent and too weak.

This path cannot be walked alone, so we must carry three people, and since we cannot go as one family, we must embrace three families, and since we cannot go as one nation, we must embrace three nations. Therefore, we understand that although we are the people of the Republic of Korea, we must love not only Korea but also Japan, the United States, and Germany. We have a responsibility to love all nations of the world, so please allow us to feel the pain of the world with our flesh and skin.

As we look at our broken state, we come to realize that the Father’s heart is filled with tears because the circumstances of many nations reach you, and their pain is your pain. Since we and they are inseparable as one body, we must realize that their sorrow is our sorrow in order to become your holy sons and daughters who can inherit the connections of heaven and earth.

Father, now in order to boast of this nation to the world, we have come to understand that we should not come out with the authority of nationalism. We have come to understand that it is not enough to bring out what the nation found in history. Therefore, we have understood that we must forget ourselves, sacrifice our families, and make our nations an altar. Therefore, please allow us to be able to wear white clothes and fulfill the responsibilities of priests who can offer new offerings. May we become children of unification who can strive to connect heavenly relationships with human relationships and to establish heavenly connections with someone.

Looking at the path of purpose, the more we feel frustrated, the more we feel pity for the suffering Father, and may we never forget the appearance of sons and daughters who can weep, even in dreams. Before we can rejoice in wearing white clothes, we must be able to dress you in heavenly garments and rejoice. We must long for the day when you can personally preside over the significant affairs of this world and weep aloud for that day to come.

I wish to be a child of unification who can sympathize with the Father’s pitiful appearance, so if there are sons and daughters who can do so, please bless them a million times over. May we be able to establish descendants who will shine forever and have the grace to rule all nations, and may we be blessed to cross that glorious peak, my Father, I earnestly hope and wish.

I have come to understand that the path of indemnity and restoration is the path of suffering. I have come to understand that it is a path that cannot be walked without tears, and that I cannot face the purpose without shedding tears, and I cannot call upon the Father without tears. When this nation and this people perish, you are the Father who bears a sorrow greater than the sorrow of the entire nation and people, and when the world perishes, you are the Father who bears a sorrow greater than that of the nations of the world. Therefore, even if we prosper that nation and that world, we understand that we cannot immediately alleviate the Father’s sorrow. Thus, we know that the Father is a pitiful and sorrowful being, the one who bore the cross of all crosses.

We, who have received you as our Father, understand that it is our misfortune not to bear the cross and that it is unfilial to not be able to secure a place to stand before countless enemies. May there be many sons and daughters who understand this within the Unification family. 

The tradition of the Unification family is the tradition that you have asserted on this earth through the historical process. We, who have pledged to follow you every day, dedicating our lives without shying away from the countless paths of suffering to establish this tradition, ask for your forgiveness for appearing before you once again without having formed a proper shape or form.

We naturally feel ashamed of our lack, but the more we think that the Father must bear the tremendous responsibility of the nation and the world perishing because of us, the more we come to realize that the Father is an unspeakably pitiful being. We, who are emotionally concerned before that Father, feel that we deserve to die a million times, but now we must become one offering and become a stone of support before your will. Thus, we must stand in a position where we can call ourselves one child who can understand your heart. 

We must find the way to be entirely offered as the offering of indemnity in that position, and we understand that this is the path of the children of unification and the path of victory. Please awaken your children scattered all over the world. If they have a heart that longs for a teacher, may they also long for the nation with that heart, and if they have a heart to be loyal to the teacher, may they be guided to become children of unification who struggle to take responsibility for the sad fate of humanity crying out.

Half of this year has passed. Now we must re-establish our face before the Father. I know that you will not forget the urgent situation of this nation and the sorrowful and pitiful state of those placed in an orphan-like situation in Asia. Therefore, we must not fall into despair. 

Even if this nation and this people perish, the world may remain, so may we become sons and daughters who can step forward and say that we will go anywhere for the Father, even if this nation perishes. Therefore, we must put forth all our hearts and fulfill our responsibilities. May this morning be a time for us to awaken and resolve anew as those who have received the national responsibilities given by the Father. 

Father, your beloved daughters from Japan have come here. Please let us know what they have felt and let them feel once again what they must do in the future. May this journey they have taken be a step that helps Japan and Asia, and may they become children who can dedicate their hearts to the holy altar of the Father until the end. 

We understand that there is a purpose to advance into Asia centered on that nation, so may this precious time be a time to pledge to fulfill the leading responsibilities before that providence. May each one be protected by the Father.
I humbly ask for your guidance, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents.  
Amen. *

3)  
Tears and Resurrection  
<Prayer> When I think of the existence of a nation throughout the historical process, I must be able to care for myself, care for my tribe, care for my nation, and care for my country. Therefore, I must reflect on what kind of relationship I have with my tribe, my nation, and my country.  
Throughout the long historical process, humans have woven history by forming deep historical connections and relationships behind that history, yet we humans have not been able to establish such connections within that history.  
When we work diligently today, we know that today’s work cannot be a practice for tomorrow. May we, who are looking forward to tomorrow's truth, become those who also draw a true picture today.  
For us, this time is precious; it is a time that determines life and death, and we must realize once again that a long history has flowed for this time. We must also understand that because of this time, the foundation of truth will ultimately be connected.  
In light of this, when I think about being on the destined path of fulfilling the purpose of history today, I cannot help but feel that our Unification Church, which exists among this, cannot escape from this historical destiny.  
Father, humans have lived by connecting such relationships and have claimed that they will pioneer the path of destiny beyond the fate they are placed in. They have lived like this and continue to live like this, and they intend to live like this in the future.  
When we see such a world, we must realize that the point they are heading towards is not a world centered on themselves where only they remain. The culmination of that relationship must be You, who are the center of the overall purpose. When we feel this, the question becomes whether all conditions can harmonize with You and whether all our words, actions, and thoughts can connect with that culmination.  
Now, if there is a son who can call You Father, is that son truly the son whom You desire and wish for in the true sense? Standing in such a position, is he a son who can call You Father? When we think about these issues, as descendants of fallen humanity, we desire to be grafted into the new son sent from the Father after crossing the hill of restoration and passing through the relationship of the two sons, and we wish to be embraced in the Father’s bosom.  
However, there are many times when we feel that the distance between us and the Father is too far. In our life journey and faith journey, there are times when we feel as if the Father is absent when we are lonely, and there are times when we think about how much the Father must struggle because of us when we are wandering.  
When we think about this, we must question ourselves whether we are truly living with the relationship of life that we promised with the Father for eternity, and how many sons and daughters can confidently say yes to that.  
Father, we do not wish to flow along with the passing history. We want to block the sorrowful history and present a joyful aspect of history by pioneering it anew. We want to present this throughout our lives and leave a practical foundation like this. This is the path that countless humans desire and must walk. However, how many people live in an environment of sorrow where they cannot realize the value of such content, and even though they pledge it, they let it flow away? When we think about this, we must feel that a land where not a single person like that exists is indeed a miserable world and a sad world.  
We must realize that the Father wishes to be on this earth, desires to fulfill one purpose with the people living on this earth, and is surely seeking someone who will fulfill that purpose. Therefore, we must question whether we are the necessary people for this era or this world today. The question is whether all our senses and emotions that we feel through our five senses are in the form that You desire and that this era needs.  
When we reflect on whether we stand in a position representing the entire universe, transcending the individual, the nation, and the world, we will feel how far we are from the Father, how much we have criticized the Father from a self-centered perspective, and how much we have demanded results based on ourselves.  
When we think about this, we come to know that the place we are in is not a place where we stand on our own but a place where we could fall. When we think about how we wanted to take pride in ourselves while standing in such a place, we must remove such images of ourselves. In the midst of this, we must realize that today is a point in time where we must find and establish a person who can rely on the Father and stand because of the Father. We earnestly wish for this realization, Father.  
Now, when we ask ourselves what kind of appearance we have before the Father, some may say they come with such sorrow, while others may claim they have come this way for such hope. There will be those who appear with something they can assert in their own way. However, how many people can say that they have fought until now centered on Your historical story and Your will? The question is how many can say they have fought and endured not just for a part of that story but for the whole. We earnestly wish for this realization, Father.  
When we call You Father, may we become sons who can make You rejoice and become sons who can hand over all Your wishes, and may we be able to meet a Father who does not feel regret while giving all His love. If You can grant us even a moment to meet such a Father, we earnestly wish for that, Father.  
In our quiet hearts, we must realize how strongly our admiration for You has arisen, and in that place where we can share life’s authority in unity with You, we must have a strong and courageous heart that can overcome any evil forces. Or, we must be in a position of strong and courageous warriors who can defeat the enemy centered on the heavenly will for the sake of enduring. We must have the authority of victory to trample on the powers of darkness and be able to maintain this living realm. When we think about this, we feel that we do not possess all these qualities. We must confess once again that we are lacking.  
We do not wish to live in sorrow while flowing along with the sorrowful history, nor do we wish to collapse due to sorrow. We earnestly ask and wish to be the representatives of a new era who can kick away the sorrowful history and establish a joyful history of the new Father. We wish for this time to be a time where we can gather to become sons and daughters who can do so.  
When asked, “Whose son are you? Whose daughter are you?” we must not hesitate. I am Your son. No matter what I see, I resemble You. What I live by is what I learned from You, and what I speak is what You taught me. The way I act like this is because You have surely encouraged me to live this way as a promise of inheritance, and all content comes from You. Everything I do, all the paths I walk, come from the Father.  
We must become the kind of person who can say this. We earnestly wish to become beings who long for a life of making a commitment before the Father with such an environment.  
Father, You are eternal, You are infinite, and You are the origin with which we can become one with You. Therefore, we earnestly wish for You to grant us an absolute connection that cannot be separated from us in eternal environments and eternal purposes, allowing us to harmonize and walk with You.  
Father, please watch over us, who call You Father once again. When You look at us with fiery eyes, we are beings who cannot be accepted before You. Seeing that the roots of sin still conquer us, we must be in a reality that can only leave sorrow for the Father. We must become those who plead hundreds of times, asking what we should do while holding onto the Father, who must turn back in sorrow.  
We must become those who can feel the loneliness, pain, sorrow, and despair while looking at the sorrowful appearance of the Father. We must be granted the understanding of how fearful such a position is, so that we can feel that such a position must not exist. We earnestly ask and wish for us to become Your sons and daughters who can feel this.  
At this time, we bow down before You. What is it that You wish to find? Is it the fruit of the heart? Is it the fruit of life? Is it the true offering that must not be absent before the highest purpose that You desire above all else in the life journey? Is it the true sons and daughters who offer this offering? Please allow us to share the desires You wish in a sincere place with us.  
From the depths of our hearts, may our sincerity arise, and may it manifest again as power, so that we can have the appearance of revival that can once again align with the Father’s will and greet the glorious new dawn. We earnestly wish for us to be sons and daughters who lack nothing, Father.  
When we think of our shameful past, we feel the inadequacy that prevents us from lifting our faces before the Father. Therefore, today, may we have hearts that rise with new faith toward the Father. So, if there are Your children who are powerless and bowed down, Father, please give them strength, extend Your hand of life, and raise a new history of creation, so that they can become sons and daughters who can affirm the hope of tomorrow. We earnestly wish for this, Father.  
Father, we earnestly wish and pray for You to protect this nation and this people. We know how earnest Your heart is to protect this nation. You have kept this nation and this people from falling into ruin through the historical process of five thousand years, and we know that this is the result of Your love, which has not allowed us to forget all the traditional culture of our people. We understand that it is because You wanted to raise a person who can love and gather people around him to fulfill Your will.  
We must realize that it is Your position that You cannot help but protect what You love, because it is a nation that You love. We must not become pitiful, unfilial children who block Your heart from loving this nation. We must not become unfaithful children.  
You are the Father who has come to this nation and this people through history, and You are the Father who has come with a heart of love, forming an unforgettable bond with this people. Therefore, we must have a heart that can love this nation as much as You wish to love it.  
Father, please resolve the sorrow of this nation’s past and grant this nation the day of liberation. We thank You for granting us the new and true blessing of connection in this end-time era. May we receive this and keep it, passing it down as a precious offering to future generations, and may we leave it as a treasure more precious than anything else, so that this nation and this people become those whom You cannot help but love forever and cannot help but embrace forever. We earnestly wish for this.  
To do this, we must become loyal patriots and virtuous women who love the nation. We must become people who live for the nation. We must become a group that fights for the nation. Father, when You ask us if we will take responsibility for these things, if we cannot take responsibility for the whole from the beginning to the end, may we at least take full responsibility for one area and say, “I will take responsibility for this area.” Please allow us to take responsibility in our respective fields. Thus, we earnestly wish for us to become sons and daughters who love the nation, Father.  
Father, this Unification group must show that they are receiving Your love on behalf of this nation and this people. Therefore, we earnestly wish for You to help us understand the true meaning of why You have called us, who are insignificant among many people. We must clearly understand how much effort You have put into establishing a single entity for this nation and this people.  
In this world, when someone has shown grace to us during lonely times, it is the way of life to repay that grace through our lives or through our descendants in our wills. We must not forget that the connection of blessing You have given to this nation and this people is something we must carry on. We must not forget that we have been sought out with a love that surpasses the love for the nation. Father, please help us realize that we are in such an era.  
This is a precious time that cannot be exchanged for this nation, nor for thirty million people, nor for the entire world. Please help us realize that this is a gift granted by You only once as the Father, and we must receive it with a grateful heart and know how to elevate its value to infinite worth. We earnestly wish for us to feel that we must become such beings at this time, Father.  
Father, please look upon Your children gathered here this morning. We must become like little children who know nothing. We must become like innocent little children who can look at the Father’s face without shame and greet Him. Thus, we must be able to see what is in Your heart that You wish to give us. We must feel it in our hearts and, longing for it, become those who can be an example before Your magnificent presence. We earnestly wish for us to become such sons and daughters, Father.  
We often become too lax. While we have the appearance of children, we often act like adults. We must become like children, so Father, at this time, please allow us to be the adorable little children who can be embraced in Your bosom. We must become little children who know nothing.  
When we are in a position where we have been hurt, or when we are in a sad place, or when we are in a lonely place, or when we find ourselves in the enemy’s territory, may we understand that Your love is intensified.
When I stand in this place, Father, I earnestly hope and wish that You will allow me to have a heart that can long for Your embrace with the heart of a child. We cannot sit here alone. We must be in a place where countless angels and ten thousand saints surround us, where the holy welcome of victory unfolds, and where we can call You Father. At this time, may You personally embrace us and welcome us as Your sons and daughters, saying, "You are the children I have been searching for." I earnestly ask and wish that each of us can accept the blessings of the gifts You have hidden in our hearts.

Father, please look upon the children of unification scattered across the nation at this time. We earnestly hope and wish that You will protect us. We know that we have not been called to this place for anyone else, but rather we have been called for You before the nation. There are those who have been betrayed by the nation for Your sake. Before the nation walks the path of suffering, we have often been the ones to walk the path of suffering according to Your will. Many of Your sons and daughters have developed wrinkles on their faces from the sorrow they have endured, which has become a habit. The wrinkles that appear on their faces must become wrinkles that can comfort You. If they cannot do so, then as they see those wrinkles, may they feel Your aching heart and be strong, courageous, and resolute wherever they go. As the time draws near, may they become those who fight until the end. I earnestly hope and wish that they will be able to comfort one another as Your sons and daughters.

We have been a group that has insisted that we must not become miserable in order to escape the nation's persecution. We have been on a path of endurance, cultivating our abilities while walking the path of restoration. Therefore, we must hold onto the rope of mercy that You extend to us, and I earnestly hope and wish that You will protect us. 

We must not trust in anything of this world, but rather we must believe only in You, and I hope that You will allow us to feel that we must stand in a place where we can yearn for the connection of life with You. If there are those who gather their hearts and offer their sincerity towards this place, which is called the homeland of life, may You grant them blessings a thousandfold and ten thousandfold. I earnestly hope and wish for this.

Father, the people here at the headquarters are before Your will, so please bless them as well. When we feel that there are not many who can stand in such a place that can become the source of life, I hope that the sincerity of those who offer their devotion for this will not block our path but rather awaken us once again at the headquarters, as we feel the fear of being judged.

If there are those who pray earnestly before You, spending the night in anguish for this nation, this people, and all of humanity, may You come upon them, Father. Please remember them. If they offer their sincerity for the path of Your will and for the sake of this world, may You recognize them as an altar where life can dwell.

Until now, You have carried the countless connections of lonely individuals throughout the history of providence, so please encourage and protect them, and guide them on their path. Father, I earnestly ask and wish for this. This morning, may their hearts think of one will, and may they focus solely on You.

I earnestly hope and wish that You will protect Your lonely children scattered across the world. We know that we have the responsibility to connect many countries in Japan and Asia, centered around Korea. However, the current state of the world is being swept into sorrow. Father, I earnestly hope that You will be the center here. We, who are well aware of the realistic environment that no one in this world can trust, must have a heart that believes only in You. May we be Your sons and daughters who can tie ourselves with ropes for fear of being separated from You, and even if trials come tomorrow, may we have a solid lifestyle that can endure and go forth.

Now, we know that there is still a long way to go on the path of the cross that the Unification Church, the Unification Nation, and the Unification World must take. Many people are willing to turn back from the path of the cross. Many are trying to avoid the path of the cross. Many are struggling to escape it through the night, but there are not many who are willing to take responsibility and walk that path. When we feel this, we come to realize that God is a sorrowful being. You must believe and walk the path of numerous historical crossroads, national crossroads, and the crossroads of life, and You cannot be a pitiful being.

For such a God, we must fulfill our duty of loyalty and our duty of filial piety, becoming loyal subjects and dutiful children. May those who respect their connection with You and step forward as a unified group become heirs who can inherit the authority of the cross. We have learned that those who inherit the cross and fulfill their responsibilities as heirs do not perish. When the cross they bore is the cross of the nation, they will seek You, Father, more earnestly than the nation they are looking for.

Therefore, today we must follow such a group. We must recognize that the name "Father" is a sorrowful one. We must understand that the stories You carry are sorrowful tales that cannot be shared with Your beloved sons and daughters. We must recognize that You are the lonely and sorrowful Father who has woven the history of providence while hiding such stories.

If anyone were to speak of the circumstances You have faced, may they become children who can feel that You seek a time when they can weep for a thousand years and give thanks for a thousand years. Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.

Now we stand within Your will. We have a relationship with You. If we did not have a relationship with You and did not belong to You, we would be a pitiful group. However, we have been those who have followed Your will for ten years or even dedicated our lives to it, so everything we have done must end in Your glory and must end in Your joy. Father, I earnestly hope and wish that You will protect us.

There are only two days left in this June. Father, please forgive us for not spending this month meaningfully. Half of the year has already passed, and the second half is approaching us. On this morning, as we carry the mission to run towards the second half of the year, may You encourage us. May we become Your sons and daughters who run towards the nation of blessings that You can leave behind, following a new connection. I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> To escape the fallen environment, we cannot choose a smooth and reasonable path. Even if humanity falls into such an environment by their own will, they cannot escape it; since they have fallen into it by external forces, they cannot escape it by their own will. This environment must be escaped from by external forces. In other words, because we have fallen into this position passively, we cannot escape from this position in a passive manner. Therefore, to traverse this path, we must engage in struggle. I cannot escape this environment by leaving it freely; I must step over the conflicting and contradictory contents that exist here. This is the position of our fallen state.

Today, we have lost heaven and lost the earth. In other words, we have lost ourselves. Because of this, we have lost all the historical content we have woven together to exist until now, and we have lost all the contemporary content we are living in today. Because of this lost past and present, we are inevitably destined to lose the future as well. Therefore, to overcome the environment that makes us lose ourselves, we must have a stronger power than the power of the past and the power of the present. Thus, the issue becomes how to discover ourselves with such power.

As we know, when we look at the history of the countless prophets who have come out to fulfill the will of heaven, they have walked the path of miserable fate. They were our historical ancestors who have guided this difficult path with their lives centered on the goal of life. However, we must understand that the path they walked ultimately led to the sorrow of the defeated. When we think of this, the fact that we are once again inheriting this historical fate and proclaiming historical victory is indeed a revolution within a revolution and cannot be a greater event than any event in history.

Then, what is the cause of all historical failures? It is not that we want to go to such a place of failure. It is because the internal power drives us to the point where we cannot help but go. All the connections of the environment pull us along. The power that drives us is greater than our own resolution and stronger than the environment we are in, which is why our ancestors repeatedly failed. We must recognize that this is the motive for failure woven by the fall.

Then, what is the origin of this motive? It is the evil that we must eliminate. What is the subject of this evil? It is the Satan that we know today. This Satan has been violating humanity, violating history, and is currently violating the 3 billion people of this world.

How do we defeat this monster that is violating humanity? It cannot be done with our own strength. Even if we seek some method or wise solution with our knowledge, it cannot be defeated. We need a power beyond our own.

Today, we have encountered the consequences of this fall not because of our own motives. We have become passive. Then, who is the subject that has placed us in this passive position? It is Satan, the enemy of God and humanity. This Satan does not stand in a position to provide us with the conditions for happiness; rather, it opposes it completely and universally.

All the opposing content is not just the materials or environmental conditions we deal with on our stage of life today. We must understand that it binds us with content that can surpass the environment, the world, and even history.

So how do we break free from such an environment? We must have a stronger new belief than all the historical connections, and we must have new abilities, new resolve, and new knowledge. What is this new knowledge, and where does this new resolve come from? It does not come from us. There must be One who is stronger than Satan. If there is an evil subject, there must be One who is stronger than that evil subject. Humanity is searching for that One. Humans must meet that One day.

That One must come with a new plan and a new countermeasure. This is the path that fallen humanity must take. We must recognize that there is no other way. Therefore, countless humans have come out seeking God.

Those who have sought the true path until now have been our ancestors who have woven history and could save the nation. Such ancestors prayed, "God, save us. God, help me."

What does God require of humanity in the course of His providential will and efforts to save humanity? He says, "Hold onto Me. Seek the way to become completely one with Me." Without seeking the way to become completely one with God, there is no way to escape this tremendous realm of death today.

Then, what is the greatest desire of humanity? If there are any desires, they must be desires that can be newly initiated in connection with God, rather than desires for oneself. We must pursue absolute values not from our own perspective, but from the perspective of being connected to the Absolute Being.

Today, fallen humanity cannot escape the connections of the fall without going through such a position. If we do not escape these connections, no matter how much we want to possess the conditions for happiness, those conditions will have nothing to do with us. We must become strong with the One who is stronger than this environment and stronger than the motive that created this environment. Otherwise, there is no way to resolve this.

Because humanity is in such a pitiful position, God is leading the history of providence to teach us such a path. Is it not the mission of religion to take responsibility as a foundation for the providence of salvation? Through religion, we must absolutize God. Even if we believe, we must believe absolutely; even if we act, we must act absolutely; and even if we fight, we must fight absolutely. By doing so, a new beginning will start. This is the necessity of seeking a solution for fallen humanity.

Therefore, if we summarize the Bible's message, it is to believe in God. We must believe in God not from any intermediate position but from an absolute position that transcends the history of East and West. God is seeking such a person. Thus, God's desire is to find a person who can believe absolutely. The same goes for believing and practicing. He is seeking a center that can present absolute actions through absolute belief and practice.

Therefore, humanity must stand in such an absolute position and act from such a position. Moreover, in living from such a position, one must not live centered on oneself but must live centered on God, living instead for God. Even if one lives and dies from such a position, it must not be for oneself but rather for God. Otherwise, we cannot escape the realm of the fall today.

If one lives for oneself and dies for oneself, they will not be able to escape the realm of death. If one lives centered on oneself, that life is a life within the realm of the fall, and thus they cannot escape that realm. Furthermore, if one's faith is within the realm of the fall, it will not transcend that realm. If one cannot transcend the realm of faith within the fall and remains connected to Satan, they cannot enter into the realm of God.
Today, we do not know how ugly, evil, and false the world we live in and the historical era we are passing through is. It is a world that is endlessly connected, no matter how much we try to sever it, and it is tangled up without end, no matter how much we try to untangle it. We must cut and untangle these things. Being within the realm of corruption, we are destined to demand absolute trust, absolute desire, and absolute love towards the absolute God.

96 Tears and Resurrection
This world does not allow me to live absolutely centered on such desires, such trust, and such love. Therefore, we must fight against the surrounding environment. This is the path that a believer must take. For this reason, today, God and we are infinitely far apart. However, we must inevitably establish a relationship with God. But how do we establish that relationship? It cannot be established by any means. We cannot establish it with the methods we have sought. It is not something that can be grasped by my own strength or by any tricks. So, what is a way to establish a close relationship? No enemy of the world should boldly and confidently come to me.

The world of Satan has continued to develop. The more we carry evil until the end of the world, the more the fallen environment of the world of Satan pushes us forward. Here, God wants to establish a relationship with humanity and says to separate from Satan, to separate from the evil world, to turn back. When we look back with connections that cannot be turned back, we find not a country that He is seeking, but a country that we are trying to escape from in our own way, a parent, a sibling, a spouse, and children. How wonderful it would be if you could turn back with all of these! You would want to turn back all at once, but you cannot turn back all at once. You must turn back one by one.

You may know the principle of restoration through indemnity. When you part from a loved one, you must turn back with tears in your eyes. You cannot turn back joyfully. When Adam and Eve fell and were expelled from God, could Adam shed tears upon seeing Eve? Could Eve shed tears upon seeing Adam? Could Adam and Eve shed tears upon seeing the archangel? No, they could not. So, when Adam shed tears of repentance, who did he center his tears on? Did he shed tears centered on Eve, or centered on the archangel? Or did he shed tears centered on God because God was saddened? No, he shed tears centered on himself. This is the essence of the fall. Adam said to Eve, "It is because you did wrong that this happened." And Eve said, "But Adam, if you had not listened to me, I would not have fallen either." They were blaming each other and shedding tears.

So, how do we restore this? We must not shed tears centered on ourselves. The path of repentance begins from a position where we can shed tears for someone more pitiful than ourselves. You must understand this.

God is also in such a position. How lonely and sad must God's heart be for losing His children? However, God thinks more about His sons and daughters who are groaning in a position of despair, forever bound by the chains of the enemy, than about His own sad position. When He looks at His sons and daughters who are groaning in such a position, He forgets all His own suffering and instead sheds tears for the fallen sons and daughters. We must understand this heart of God as our Father.

To return to our original position,
So, what must we do first to escape from the sorrowful position where Adam and Eve fell and return to our original position? It is necessary to grieve over being in a position unacceptable to God as a traitor, but we must also recognize that there are many people who are more pitiful than ourselves. I am pitiful, but I must be able to shed tears for those who are more pitiful than me and for the world of humanity. We must have a sincere heart to sympathize with them and to want to save them.

Thus, even if I shed tears a thousand times for the world, the nation, and the people, this is what I must do, and even if I face loneliness ten thousand times, this is what I must endure. Let us do this in place of our past tears. If there is someone who can do this, God will be with that person.

98 Tears and Resurrection
Today, when we repent, we see that we are repenting to go to heaven. John the Baptist also said, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand." But what should we first repent for? We must repent for the nation. Even if the kingdom of heaven is near, the one who will welcome us in heaven is the one who cares for the nation. Those who cannot pray for this nation cannot be saved to heaven.

For this reason, we should not live our faith for ourselves. Such faith does not establish a nation. Such faith does not form a global nation. God's providence of salvation is to save nations.

Since the fall began with the tears of individuals, today we must possess the privileged gift of resurrection that allows us to return with tears of repentance. Otherwise, we cannot be saved. Therefore, today, we must not be those who shed tears for ourselves. Even if we are shackled for committing many sins in the world, we must be those who shed tears for our nation and for our country.

I may be in a position of ruin, but O nation! O people! Do not become like me! I must be able to shed tears. A person who sheds tears wishing that there will be no bitter and resentful experiences like theirs in the path that the nation takes can survive. A person who holds onto the sacred hope of the nation and continues on the path of death can be saved as long as the nation does not perish, even if he is a sinner.

When Jesus was to carry the cross and walk the path of death, He said, "Abba Father, not my will, but yours be done." What is the Father's will? It is to establish a holy world. The life he lived and the value of his life were not centered on himself. Although he was in a situation where he was being oppressed within the realm of the Israelite nation, he shed tears and struggled with the world while envisioning a future world that could be welcomed.

Even if we live on this earth and our lives are difficult and hard, we must be able to say, "I am like this, but you must not be like this." The central person should not insist on doing things according to his own will. If you want to care for the nation, you must not think of yourself first, and if you want to care for the nation, you must not think of your parents first, or you will not be blessed.

From this perspective, we must greet the authority of resurrection with tears of repentance. In other words, we must escape from the realm of death with tears of repentance. Life is singular, and even if one claims to have faith that does not spare any means to escape from the realm of death, he cannot escape. We must shed tears that Adam and Eve could not shed in order to break free.

We must not have the mindset of blaming others, saying, "The motive for my sin is because of you. I would not have done this if it were not for you." We must not have a mindset of being positive and normal. We must deny ourselves and affirm our environment. We must hope for the nation to be saved rather than for ourselves to be saved, and we must be able to shed tears for our family to be saved.

Those who wish to die will live, and those who wish to live will die.
Today, whether it is Christianity or numerous other religions, why are they gradually perishing as the end approaches? It is because they have lost their nation. All their prayers morning and evening are for their own blessings. They are all praying to create their own God. So when will they become the God of the nation and the God of the world? If we analyze the content of God's tears, it is not that He sheds tears for Himself.

He sheds tears to save us and to restore us. When we know that there is a God who saves us and does not shed tears only for ourselves but sheds tears for the nation and the environment, that is where God begins to work.

There may be times when you experience tears flowing like a waterfall for no reason, overwhelmed by sorrow. We must understand that sorrow. That sorrow is not our own sorrow. It is, in fact, historical sorrow. Who brings that sorrow? God brings it. So, for whom is that sorrow? It is not for God but for us. Ultimately, it is sorrow for our salvation. It is not just for my own salvation but for the salvation of the nation and the world. Without a nation, we cannot be saved. You must understand this.

That is why Jesus said, "Do not worry about what you will eat, what you will drink, or what you will wear. For the pagans run after all these things, and your heavenly Father knows that you need them. But seek first his kingdom and his righteousness." Even when we repent, we must hold onto the nation and repent, and we must hold onto the world and repent. This people stands before the will, but what should this nation do? This village stands before the will, but what should this village do? Thinking about these things and staying up all night, the person who offers sincere devotion to that village, even if that village does not accept him, can silently occupy another village. You must understand that this is the only way for God and humanity to establish a relationship.

From this perspective, when we think about Jesus, what was His lifestyle like? Even when Jesus ate, at the moment He faced the meal, He looked towards the nation through that meal. The same goes for when He spoke. His words were not for the sake of sustaining His own life but were for the purpose of fulfilling the will of the world.

Everyone wants to be a filial son or daughter, a loyal subject or virtuous woman. However, no matter how much one wants to be a filial son, a person who thinks only of himself cannot be a filial son. If one sheds tears because his clothes are not as good as his siblings', that is not being a filial son. Would there be a filial son who protests to his parents because he is worse off than his siblings? The same goes for loyalty. Is there a loyal subject who betrays the king and the nation just because he finds himself in a more miserable situation than the nation's miserable fate?

To become a true filial son, one must have a heart that cares for his siblings. Even if he sheds tears, he must shed them with the heart of caring for his siblings rather than for himself. He must be able to shed tears for his siblings who cause worry to his parents with a heart that feels sorry for them. If he stands in such a position, the parents cannot help but recognize him as a filial son. He must not think of himself first.

For this reason, religion must transcend the limits of the nation and the aspirations of humanity. In other words, it must go beyond the limits of humanity's desires and reach the point of God's desires. We must not remain at the limit of the desires of fallen humanity.

Anyone who knows the will and knows God will pray, "I do not need to be saved. Please save the world and save my nation." This is the kind of tears we must shed, for our people, for our nation, and for all humanity.

Then, for the salvation of this nation, this country, and all humanity, who will be on God's side? Completion of Resurrection 
Today, we are destined to resurrect. So what kind of resurrection must we achieve? Even if an individual resurrects, the family must also resurrect. And even if a family resurrects, the tribe must resurrect; even if the tribe resurrects, the nation must resurrect; and even if the nation resurrects, the world must also resurrect. And even if the world resurrects, it is of no use unless God is resurrected. 

Therefore, in our Unification Church today, we are setting a great purpose of world resurrection with the connection of loyalty in the place representing the nation centered on God and the connection of filial piety in the place representing the individual. 

Thus, we must shed tears and repent to achieve this purpose. This cannot be completed in a year. The sins of the nation cannot be forgiven with just a year of tears. However, we must not retreat saying, "I don’t know about God or anything else." If we do, ten years and twenty years will pass by. 

That is why Christianity has been shedding tears for the past two thousand years. Among the countless people who have shed tears, many have repented for the individual and have strived to find the ideal of individual heaven. 

However, God has sent special prophets in each era who would sacrifice and save for the individual, and they have become representatives who can connect history by caring for God, the world, the nation, and the people. 

From this perspective, when we look at history until now, we can see that a global era has arrived before us. The world today is transcending the era where any nation or any country can be centered and guided. The entire world is proclaiming a new world. Now the whole world must become one. Therefore, the time has come to propose a method of salvation centered on a specific nation. 

We, who were born in this era that can lead the salvation of the world, are blessed people.

Because we have entered this era, all our lives must transcend the walls of the world. This is a sad fact.
