We must recall the past when we shed tears for this poor nation and people. Remembering the old days when we stayed up all night shedding tears for this nation and people, we must have a more earnest heart than any patriot’s tears, and those are stories that only the Father knows. I sincerely hope and wish that those sufferings will not be led by the enemy’s grasp.

Having passed through the miserable 1960s, we have entered the 1970s. Now, this nation, the Republic of Korea, must not fall into the grave of an abandoned orphan. We must stand in the position of priests who can support that and, while staying up all night with sincerity to protect the altar, inherit the Father’s heart of concern and become children who can shed tears for the blessing of the world. We must think about how many children of unification have been entrusted with such a priestly duty.

It is not a problem that we love the Republic of Korea. We must prepare the internal connection that you had when you came to find this people so that you can pave the way to go toward tomorrow with this people. There, we must become true priests who can offer the altar of the nation before you. When we feel that there are still no such priests, we realize that the existing denominations today are in a position where you cannot trust them.

You know well that many spiritual groups have appeared. Among them, who is going forward anew? They celebrated the summer feast before we came and welcomed the autumn feast. While they welcomed summer and autumn, we were in the cold winter feast. The position of 23 degrees south latitude does not fall into the winter feast even if the sun is in the opposite realm, and we have always lived within the tropical and temperate zones, bumping against that boundary. However, at some point, when we welcome a summer day, we will know that a unifying fortune can fill heaven and earth.

Many denominations that have come and gone in history have stopped at the summer feast or the autumn feast. However, our Unification Church must go through the winter feast. When we look at the world’s civilization today, it has not gone through the civilization of spring, summer, and autumn to meet the civilization of winter. The current democratic world, boasting of the 20th century, is centered on the tropical civilization of summer and is within the temperate civilization of spring.

In front of such a world, the communists are shouting about civilization, and this false civilization moving around the Siberian plains is invading at this time, just as the Unification Church is internally groaning in the winter feast today. The Unification Church has walked a miserable path in the time of communist dominance. The communists have been driven out of this land, but the Unification Church has been welcomed. However, the Father has already informed us that this winter feast will pass and a new spring feast will come.

In this 1970s, when we can welcome the holy spring feast, Korea is pursuing a revival of religion to meet the external spring and summer feasts, so please allow the internal spring and summer feasts to align. I am concerned that we have not yet reached such a position. Father, please watch over the path of this nation.

We have the responsibility to bind the 30 million people who are divided on the 3,000-ri peninsula, fighting each other like enemies, into one brotherly bond before you, and we have realized that fulfilling that responsibility is an extremely difficult path. Furthermore, since the Republic of Korea must remain for the love of the world, we believe that we have the responsibility to expand the foundation of love globally and connect it to the world of death.

The Unification Church has developed up to now, receiving the nation’s condemnation since the time this nation did not know. When we think about how pitiful and miserable the path we have taken to lay the global foundation has been, sometimes we hear all the news from those responsible for the nation, and all the sons and daughters sitting here know that the Father’s sorrow is scattered everywhere.

In a wasteland overflowing with the waves of death, who will take on the responsibility to find the food of grace for the lonely life wandering in a desert without an oasis? If I do not do it, I know well that the Father has done it. The more I think that the foundation is connected to your hard work, the more I must realize that we at the Unification Church headquarters have the responsibility to love that nation with tears.

When they are lonely, they long for the heart of the teacher, and when they are sad, they call upon you. For whom did they come out? They came out with the heart to serve someone other than themselves, and before serving their own country, they came out to serve the world. I know that there is no fortune of destruction where such a heart is felt. That is why we have sent the lonely ones abroad and have been fighting to leave a heavenly connection with them until now. Also, since you must establish a connection with them, I feel that they are all pitiful beings.

Why must the Father be in such a position? Why must He stand in a position centered on such sons and daughters? However, we must think that the Father, who could not help but plan such providence, is the only one who is pitiful, the only one who is lonely, and the only one who is wronged. We must realize that fact. We must become sons and daughters who, feeling this sad and miserable story deeply in our bones, as if all our arteries are about to burst, are struggling without a place to report this fact, Father, I earnestly hope and wish for us to be such.

Father, now that June has passed, looking at your will, the future shines with the light of hope. I am afraid that we may not be able to become those who pledge for a vigorous tomorrow. However, even if the external appearance is like this, our internal heart is drawing closer to you, so please have mercy on that heart.

The path of the Unification Church is a thorny path that we must cover with our bodies to stop the bleeding of the altar of the blood you left behind. I earnestly ask and wish that we may become a group that will wipe away the wounds of your sorrow by covering that thorny path with our bodies.

We must long for the Father to the point of being blinded by longing. We must hold onto the pitiful Father, feeling the deep heart of the Father whom we must liberate, and say, “I have come to comfort you.” May we become those who can serve and comfort you. Thus, I earnestly ask and wish that you will personally establish a connection so that we can each have you as our Father.

Father, now June has passed. As we think of the day six months ago when we pledged for a victorious unification front, we are a group of unification that must reach out to Asia and the world, so please watch over our situation.

Even if our appearance, carrying this ideology and will, is that of a poor person in tattered clothes, may we be able to comfort you, and may we become your children who cannot leave your embrace as sons of truth, co-workers who cannot be untangled from your story. I earnestly hope and wish for this. (The following is not recorded.) *

Our Attitude
<Prayer> Loving Father! Today is the first Sabbath of July. May the new grace and blessing of this morning remain upon us.

We know that humans, who have a destiny to come once to this earth, must also bear the life responsibilities that require various paths of indemnity. Some people go east, some west, some south, and some north, each pioneering the path of destiny given to them, and we know that most people are struggling to live centered on themselves.

In this land where no one discusses their path with you, we have realized that you have held us and followed that direction, coming through individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world until now.

We must indemnify the neglect that the ancestors who have come and gone in history have shown toward you in our generation. We must feel once again that we have the mission to become the descendants you desire.

Even though you have endured that tremendous and laborious path until now, Father, you must still endure the struggle of patience. As you have pioneered the path of the suffering cross, we think of the position of the Father, who cannot even speak of such circumstances. That position must not only be connected to us but also to countless nations, and it must be connected not only to the present but also to the future, as you have come out as the central responsible person in the history of suffering until now.

While facing such a Father, we, who were born as fallen descendants on this earth, tend to want to entrust our difficulties to you and to inherit our joys as our own. When we think of this, we must reflect once again on whether we can be accepted before the Father, and each of us must realize that we are in a position of unfilial descendants.

We must feel how great the sorrow hidden in the heart of the hardworking Father is, and we must empathize with the pain of pioneering the path of the cross that you have borne. When we stand in such a position, we will know that there has been a historical flow of tears before the name of the Father, and there have been twists and turns where life and death have crossed.

We must feel a sense of shame that we cannot contain ourselves just by hearing the name of the Father. We often call upon the Father with our mouths, saying that the Father’s wish is our wish, but when it comes to the overall content of the Father, we often find ourselves in a position where we do not take responsibility.

If we are the sons of the Father, we must inherit the entirety of the Father so that we can take responsibility even in the absence of the Father. However, when we think that we have a relationship as sons yet are insufficient to pass on all the crosses, we must realize that the name of the Father is a name of a very sorrowful position.

When we call upon the Father in heaven, we must know how much suffering He has endured and that every time He sent countless prophets and saints to their death for the sake of saving this land, He has endured more pain than they did. We must learn to understand this.

Even if the enemy is filled with resentment, we must know that there is a story of the Father who cannot repay that enemy as an enemy, and there has been a heartfelt journey of the Father seeking lost sons and daughters.

Father! Please remember your little children gathered this morning. We must reflect once again on what our own appearance is. We must know that the past is the self that has lived like this, the present is the self standing in this position, and the future is the self that must become like this.

In the past, I was a sorrowful self, but in reality, there must be something that you can have hope in and be joyful about. When we think about whether we have become the kind of person that you can entrust with such a mission, we must earnestly hope to recognize what position we are in.

Thus, even if I stand in any direction among the east, west, south, and north from the Father’s side, when the Father looks in that direction and remembers and gazes upon me, a path of hope will open there. The Father’s heart of hope will also remain there. We must strive to find ourselves who can be granted such a position. We must strive to establish ourselves.

We must not become those who say they love the Father yet cannot live centered on the Father, nor should we be in a position of serving ourselves while saying we serve the Father. Please help us to clearly realize this, Father, and I earnestly hope and wish for it.
Jesus appeared before Peter and asked, "Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?" Peter replied, "Yes, Lord, you know that I love you." However, when Jesus asked again, Peter could not help but feel hesitation in his heart, and by the third question from Jesus, he was in a position where he could not lift his face due to shame.

Reflecting on Peter's situation, where he could not look Jesus in the eye and had to respond again, we too sometimes find ourselves in such positions. When the Father asks, "Do you love me?" we find ourselves unable to answer that we love Him, even though we know that He knows our hearts. Despite feeling inadequate and unworthy of His love, how often do we cry out in prayer, desperately asking Him to love us?

In response to the question of whether we love Him, we are in a position where we cannot answer confidently, yet we forget the Father's position and stand in a place centered around ourselves, acting as unfilial children. We must realize that regardless of our situation, we should be able to care for the Father's heart.

We need to understand the Father's worried heart. Even if we face destruction, we should be able to rise above our circumstances to prevent blocking the path of the Father's sorrow, and even if we cannot be the perfect filial children who can overcome the mountain of death, we should at least strive to imitate them. I earnestly hope and desire that we can feel this once again at this moment.

I know that this place holds the tremendous name of the Unification Church. It is not the number of people that makes it great, but because it is a place where the anchor of the Father's heart can be lowered. This is a precious place where life and death can be determined, and the origin of life can be established, making it a place we cannot call anything less than great.

Father, just as a prisoner standing in court waits for the judge's verdict with all his heart, how many of your sons and daughters gathered here can feel that same sentiment? When asked how serious we are about your will and how serious we are about you, how many of us can answer confidently? The future path of the church can be measured by how we answer these questions, and we must recognize how fearful our positions and circumstances are.

Father, this morning, please steady our hearts. We are ashamed to even ask to be embraced in your holy grace. If you had not bestowed your holy grace upon us, we would not have been able to receive blessings from the world of death, nor would we have been able to escape the realm of death and suffering. When we think of this, we must call out to you even in death, and even if we face destruction, we must call out to you, and even while being beaten, we must hold onto your hand.

When a parent strikes a beloved child with a whip, it is not the whip that is frightening, but the fact that love and love are intertwined in that act. The child being beaten does not understand this. When we consider that those who repeatedly find themselves in positions of rebuke have left countless rebellions in history because they did not understand the heart of the parent, we must realize that we, as the descendants of fallen ancestors, must inherit the heart of a parent's love even in such situations. When we think of this, we must be able to submit to that position and be willing to accept the whip a million times.

When the Father cries out, "Who will bear the lonely cross of the heavenly family?" how many sons and daughters will step forward humbly in white robes, willing to become a holy offering drenched in blood? When the Father asks such questions, I earnestly hope and desire that there will be many heavenly sons and daughters here who can boldly say that they have sought the path to be able to do so.

It is not a matter of quantity, but I know that there is a way for one filial child to comfort the heart of a parent with unfilial children. Therefore, Father, please take our Unification family as a holy foundation where you can rest. This is the wish of your son and the path he desires.

Father, please place your sons and daughters gathered here in a position that you can call holy. May they become sons and daughters who carry the history with content that cannot be ignored by the countless saints of the heavenly world. To do this, may they be willing to make all sacrifices from a public standpoint and bear all difficulties, becoming offerings for you.

Now, we have passed the first half of 1970. Today marks the first Sabbath of July as we embark on the remaining half of the year. We must shed the shameful posture we had when facing the Father and repent once more for our past unfilial behavior. In the upcoming second half, we must be able to declare that we will become sons and daughters whom you can trust, who can receive your heartfelt stories. Even if everyone else cannot, may we be able to prostrate ourselves before you, struggling and earnestly dedicating ourselves.

We know that time flows away without notice. The path of suffering we walked in the 1960s has passed, and now half of the 1970s has also gone by. We understand that our start this year is precious. We must bind together the source of power that can move the entirety of the 1970s through this year, and we must possess the essence of all good motives so that we can bear good fruit every year in the 1970s. When we think of the responsibility that lies upon us, we earnestly ask that you take charge of the remaining 1970s, fill our hearts with a deep longing for heaven, and let the desire to cry out to meet you explode within us.

We know that in a place where we long to meet each other, we can begin to share. When the bonds of connection deepen, the bonds of giving and receiving also deepen. May we clearly understand the Father's teaching to strive to meet one another in the end.

When a person forgets themselves and thinks of many others, that person becomes the center of those people, which is the traditional connection of history and the traditional path toward goodness. Therefore, I earnestly hope and desire that your sons and daughters will be able to sacrifice for many people and accumulate merit for many people in public positions.

On this day, this morning, the members of the Unification Church scattered around the world will be gathering their hearts toward Seoul, the center of the Republic of Korea, offering their prayers and looking forward to the day they will meet again. May infinite love be with them. Though they are limited by distance and materially constrained, their hearts are not limited, and they are filled with a deep longing. However, if there are family members who are shedding tears before you due to the circumstances that prevent them from meeting, please appear and personally comfort them, and give them your instructions. Knowing that there will be many difficulties in overcoming the remaining path of suffering, may you gently guide them so that they can find a resting place and stand as glorious children.

Father, they must fight against the great realm of death placed before humanity as they walk the path of restoration. When we consider that this responsibility must be removed through struggle, even if it must be torn away by mouth, they are a group that cannot help but be pitied, so I earnestly ask you to remember them.

Among your sons and daughters scattered throughout South Korea, if there are those who gather their hearts toward Seoul this morning, admiring your holiness and pledging their connection with you, longing to have a moment of glory that can shine tomorrow, may you bless them a thousandfold, ten thousandfold.

The place we are looking at has been a tedious place. The place of prayer has been a path of suffering. You know this well, so please be on their side. May your love be upon them as they fulfill their stories and wishes. Furthermore, may you directly manifest and place them in a position where they can boast of having had a joyful moment in their lives, connecting them with the opportunity to be guided directly by you.

If there are sons and daughters who long for this place but cannot attend this morning, may you bestow the same blessings upon them, and may your holiness accompany the remaining time.

As we pray for the nation, pray for the world, and pray for the path of this altar we must walk with you, please accept all our prayers with joy. You know well the specific contents we are praying for, so I earnestly ask that you fulfill them according to your will, allowing us to surely meet a moment of glory on this land.

At this time, I earnestly ask that your glory and grace connect with the hearts and bodies of your sons and daughters gathered in various places. Please personally oversee all of this. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Today, we are well aware that we are the descendants of the fallen. It is true that individuals in society remain in such positions, and families, tribes, nations, and the world remain in such positions. We also know that our lives today are about finding the path of morality that must rise above these circumstances.

The path a believer must take
However, the environment before us does not contain anything that can harmonize with us and provide our hopes. Although we live within it, it does not allow us to harmonize with one another or open our hearts. We understand that this is due to the fall. Therefore, it is pitiful that we, who must be born, live, and die within such circumstances, are in such a plight. However, despite having a pitiful fate, we must seek a life path that allows us to walk the path of hope without being pitiful. The question is whether we can resolve to not be pitiful ourselves, even in such a pitiful environment.

If we have new hopes or aspirations in our lives today, we must be able to establish connections for a happy self that can overcome our pitiful selves so that those hopes do not become pitiful hopes but rather happy hopes. Otherwise, those hopes cannot manifest as joy. The question of how a person overcomes and transcends their environment is not limited to the individual but is a societal issue that emerges and, furthermore, a global issue. This is the current state of affairs.

Politicians are deeply concerned with how to transform the unfortunate fate of the nation into a happy one centered around their politics. They strive to find connections that can become the content of happiness. Similarly, religious leaders must also pursue happiness and hope from an awakened standpoint, even in an unhappy world environment. Therefore, we are well aware that we continue to fight at the boundary of how the recognized self engages with the conditions of happiness by negating all current circumstances and environments.

Even if, through such struggles, we establish conditions for joy centered around a certain connection in a moment, that connection cannot replace one's entire life and history. Compared to the environment, that connection is far too small. Thus, the joy obtained through that small connection is once again eroded by the environment and is repeatedly conquered by the connections of the environment, a reality we experience in our daily faith lives. Therefore, fallen humans cannot help but struggle on the path to finding the truth.

So, how can we leave behind conditions of happiness or hope in our lives amidst this unhappy environment and maintain them as the center of our lives? This is a question that is of utmost importance to believers.

When God seeks a place to rest on this earth, He cannot come to an unhappy place. Likewise, when heavenly fortune comes to this earth, it cannot come to an unhappy environment. When happiness and hope dwell on this earth, that happiness and hope must not only be for a moment but must be able to dwell eternally beyond that life. When there is a foundation for such connections, the God who exists eternally will come to that foundation of happiness. The heavenly fortune centered on that eternal foundation can also come only when such conditions are established.

A believer must have an unchanging heart
Considering this, the path of faith is one that centers around the heart, and no religion teaches believers to change their hearts. They teach that one must have an unchanging heart. The heart one held ten years ago must not change ten years later, and even if time passes and life ends, that heart must remain unchanged. If a religion teaches this, it is a true religion.

There must be a foundation of an unchanging heart. That foundation of an unchanging heart must exist not for the sake of what can change, nor should it aim for something that can change, but it must exist for what does not change and must look toward an unchanging goal. How to establish that foundation of heart is the most important issue for believers. That foundation of heart becomes the origin of life that cannot be exchanged for anything. From here, believers must realize the value of their faith lives, that is, the original posture must be established.

Such connections should not be bound to just one person but should expand the environment centered around oneself. There, one must accelerate several times and broaden those connections in all directions. Through oneself, the eternal...
The extent to which the environment has developed as a condition for happiness becomes the foundation of blessings that a person can possess in the heavenly world and is undoubtedly the origin of happiness. Therefore, in pioneering this path, the happiness sought by people in today's world cannot be found. It is hopeless. This is because this world is a realm of death, and all desires pursued in harmony with this world, which exists in the realm of death, are fundamentally at odds with the eternal aspirations that we seek based on our original state.

As the external environment expands, the influence of that external breath fundamentally conflicts with the internal and essential foundation of happiness that we must seek, which can last forever. Thus, we must understand that as external conditions increase, the internal aspects decrease in inverse proportion. To escape this realm of death created by our fall, we must completely sever external environments. Therefore, the issue becomes how to create the desired realm as a whole and how to develop the internal connections that can last forever, which is why there are many restrictions on the path of believers. We must recognize that there are many burdens that are difficult to bear.

However, these restrictions are not meant to bind us. There is a difference between the front and back of these restrictions. While the front is swept by the waves of death, the back begins to see the waves of life starting to rise. We must understand that there is a stark contrast between the enormous waves of death raging outside and the subtle waves of life beginning to rise within. Therefore, living while guarding against the waves of death cannot be a lonely endeavor. You must understand that this cannot be a pitiful situation.

However, just because it is lonely does not mean we can forget or avoid that loneliness. We must recognize that we are in a position where we must defend this lonely place and the place of suffering. If we were to leave this position, the waves of death, like a raging tide trying to swallow that loneliness, would wash away the waves of our lives without a trace. This is the struggle between the front and back of humanity living today. Therefore, we can feel that our hearts cannot rest for a moment and are trembling in the world of fear and struggle. The stronger the desire to truly walk the path of heaven becomes, the more we will feel that the heavenly aspirations sprouting strongly within our deep hearts will capture us in infinite fear.

When a relative entity appears in this heart, the shape of Satan, who has violated history, may also appear. Thus, a battle between the realm of death and the realm of life unfolds. As we unknowingly fight in that place, when we feel it and commit our entire lives to it, it manifests in form, and spiritual experiences occur.

I must hold onto God. Here, I am in an extremely weak position, while on the contrary, evil is in an extremely strong position. The position of good is merely a single point. For example, if you touch a point on the surface of water with your finger and then remove it, that point will be occupied by the water again as soon as your finger is removed. Similarly, the foundation of joy that arises in our hearts is just a single point, like putting a finger in water. As soon as you remove your finger from the water, the water immediately occupies that spot, and the forces of evil that seek to occupy it all at once attack from all sides, which a person living a spiritual life will experience.

Therefore, to not lose that standard of good, one must devote their heart, will, and character. This is essential. It is from the position of giving everything that eternity begins; there can never be eternity from a moderate, halfway position. Thus, if we continue to remain in a halfway state, we will inevitably end within the realm of death. We must go beyond the intermediate position that belongs to this realm of death and give our all.

In doing so, we are not limited to the instinctive or physical limits we were born with. We need conditions that allow us to say we have given beyond those limits. Therefore, we must stand in the position of saying, "O God! Please help me. My strength and ability are insufficient; O God, please help me." Then, because God has the power to help, by giving our all along with that power, we can surpass the limits of our own strength. You must understand that only then will God place our lives on the line and make a new start.

When Jesus came to this earth and proclaimed the gospel, he spoke revolutionary words. What were they? He said to love me more than anyone else. If you do not love me more than your own child or wife, you cannot be my disciple and are not worthy of me. Furthermore, he said that unless you carry your own cross and follow me, you cannot be my disciple. You must carry your own cross.

What kind of cross is that? It is a double-sided cross. Standing in an isolated position swept by the waves of death, one must hold onto God and fight against the great with the small. To maintain my small self against the great that arises from the connections of the realm of death, the power of God, which has been pushing me away from the waves of death until now, must be like a wall behind me. Without that, I will be swept away without mercy, so I must hold onto God firmly.

By taking my small movements as a motive and not retreating, when I break through the line of death, God will push me forward with the power to follow along, and through me, the connections of evil will be conquered. The path of coming out of such connections is the path of restoration. Since humanity has fallen, restoration must also be carried out by humanity, and you must understand that this is how the standard is established.

When a typhoon blows in, go to the sea once. Think about how much the sailor on a boat that is overcoming the waves of the sea due to the storm must be anxious. Overcoming such a level is the path of faith. When you realize that the last hurdle threatening your life is not the only one, but that higher and greater waves are continuously coming, the farther you go from land, the more you cannot help but feel the threat to life and experience fear. A believer walking the path of faith is like the sailor anxiously steering the boat to avoid the fate of capsizing amidst the raging waves, isn't it? You must understand that the path of faith we are walking today is such a path.

When you speak of God's providence of restoration, it may seem simple. In this Korea, the hand of God's providence of restoration is connected. Moreover, the hand of God's providence of restoration extends to various countries around the world. Today, when looking at Korea as the center, Korea is merely a point among the many countries of the world. To carry out the providence of restoration centered on a country in such a position, that country must have a time of connection where numerous evil nations invade, and thus it cannot help but be swept away by such waves.

When looking at the Republic of Korea, there are numerous ethnic groups. Among these numerous ethnic groups, there are countless individuals. I am one person among those countless individuals. The global evil fortune that is sweeping in from the outside does not come with a historical limit but is creating waves centered on the connections of our daily lives. That time is precisely now.

In this context, when considering myself connected to a certain ethnic group in the Republic of Korea, think about how far the world of victory and hope I must traverse is. Today, I must not simply live in this position. What we must do as we walk that path is to equip ourselves with the authority to govern all creation as the sons of God.

Then, what does it mean to be the lord of all creation? Who is the lord of all creation? Today, people say it is humanity, but the fundamental lord of all creation is God. Isn't that so? You know that there is a spirit. Humans have that spirit. Since humans are the leaders among spirits, they are ultimately connected directly to God, which is why they are called lords.

Being the lord of all creation cannot be achieved solely by humanity. Since humans are also creations, how can they become the lord of all creation? A created being is a relative result. Simply being a created being cannot allow one to access or occupy the cause. Created beings are destined to be occupied by the cause. You are undoubtedly a result-oriented existence. When you become a lord, the term "lord" means the center among spirits. This means that it refers to the original relationship where God and humanity are united.

How complicated is the position of the Republic of Korea today? Is the place where you can rest as individuals within the borders of the Republic of Korea? Where would that be? Would it be Japan or China? This is a significant issue. When you ask where your resting place is, is it within the Republic of Korea? It cannot be limited to just within the Republic of Korea. While the Republic of Korea is necessary in the position restored to heaven through new transformation, the current Republic of Korea itself cannot be the foundation of victorious restoration or a resting place for the world.

So, what must be done to have a resting place for the restoration of the world? You must understand that it is necessary to overcome the global path of suffering. Therefore, those who wish to become sons and daughters of God must not have a sincere effort limited to the borders of the Republic of Korea. Such individuals may be sons and daughters of God within the borders of the Republic of Korea, but they cannot stand as representatives before the entire nation of God.

Thus, the lord must connect with God. However, not everyone is a lord just because humanity is the lord of all creation. There are those who can become lords. The qualifications to join that club of lords are at least not for the sake of individuals. They live for the whole. God seeks to fulfill that desire centered on such individuals. When that happens, whose kingdom will it be? It will not be God's kingdom but that person's kingdom.

God has come through a long historical process to promote the providence of restoration and has come to the Unification Church in the Republic of Korea not to remain within the Unification Church in the Republic of Korea. Therefore, it is essential to lead this denomination and to reach the position of being the center of the world. To do that, we must overcome all the waves of death that come crashing in. Only then can we become the origin of heaven that can remain within the realm of death, equipped with all the methods and tools to defend this side even when we cross over to the other side.

However, we are still in a position where we must cross the river without having reached the intended destination, so when the river is tormented by raging tides or storms, we ourselves are also tormented while crossing the river. There can be no eternal rest here. Jesus came to this earth in such a position. Therefore, the significance of his return also holds meaning in this context.

The Unification Church must achieve victory centered on both spirit and flesh. Although Jesus was sacrificed within the realm of death, he established the origin of the realm of life through his resurrection. When that origin connects beyond the global limits and is linked to the heavenly kingdom, he must return to the world of death with that content to welcome the bride, for only then can there be glory and victory. However, this did not happen during Jesus' time. So, what does Christianity hope for today? Ultimately, it hopes to welcome the Lord who is coming, for the sake of entering the heavenly kingdom.

Today, individuals belonging to the Unification Church in the Republic of Korea are in a personal position, but that individual can represent the Unification Church, the Republic of Korea, and the world. That individual must possess a value that can overcome the global realm of death. When that happens, wherever that person stays becomes heaven. Anywhere is heaven.

As you walk the path of faith centered on the Unification Church, you will feel the tremendous waves of fear and indifference crashing in front of you, even if you do not know what lies ahead. The question is how to overcome and pass through these waves. When we are defenseless before the incoming waves, everything will be shattered.

So, what must we possess here? We need something that can serve as a resting place, a place where we can drop anchor in the gospel. No matter how much I can move back and forth, in my current position, I can only move left and right; I cannot move forward and backward. I stand on a path of fate where I can advance but cannot retreat. Not only can I not retreat, but as time goes on, those who do not have the connections to advance will have no way to overcome the incoming fear. Here, we should not worry about the fear but rather have the vitality to pull the lifeline that allows us to live beyond that fear. By doing so, we can use that as a stimulus of hope to surpass the fear. When that happens, you must understand that hope begins to emerge in the path ahead. Then, will not God, who looks upon that, reconsider?

You must understand that the path of faith is not a path of retreat. The path of faith is not a path of retreat but a path that must be walked by combining left and right, which is why one cannot walk alone and needs someone to support them. Since one cannot know alone, they need friends and teachers to guide them.

Therefore, you must know who is ahead of you and who can be relied upon as a comrade beside you. A person without a comrade who can comfort them from the side is a lonely person, and a person who cannot have someone who goes ahead and teaches them while looking back is also a very pitiful person.

If there is someone who has come to this earth and has split the waves of death for humanity, who would that be? It is not the Messiah of Israel, who is called the only begotten Son of God, but rather Jesus, the Messiah of the world. He came to overcome the hardships of suffering centered on spirit and flesh, yet the historical nation’s realm of death swallowed Jesus. Therefore, he paved the way to cross the tumultuous sea of the spiritual realm of death as the victorious prince of that nation. Thus, by simply following him, one can enter the world of spiritual happiness. This has been the thought of Christianity until now.

However, today our Unification Church is not only that but also centered on both spirit and flesh...
We must go towards the place of victory where the blood is sprinkled, the cradle of rest. This is the fateful path of the Unification Church that we must long for today and tomorrow. You are also on the same fateful path.

The one and only path to save lives
So how should you go? You must clearly know what the lifeline is and hold on to it tightly. You must be able to say that this is something you cannot let go of. You must keep this in mind. It is a path you cannot choose not to take; if you try not to go, you will be in trouble. It is a path where threats come all at once, and you must understand that this is the way God and Satan are deciding.

You must hold on to this tightly. You cannot just hold it with your hands; you must bind it to your body. Thus, you must pull on this lifeline. Even if you pull on that lifeline and cannot move forward, you must keep your eyes wide open and at least focus on the direction. You cannot do otherwise. And you must wait until there is any signal from that place. You must have a fervent heart wishing for any command to come, hoping for God's grace to descend. In the final place where you cry out to God with a desperate heart, God will give you a new signal.

In following God's command to take certain measures in such a place, there is no room for doubt. Here, there is only practice. Only practice is the way to live. You must understand that only practicing can be the motivation to touch the principles of life. Various circumstances are not the issue. It is not about the connection between you and me. It is a decision that this path can go straight with God's command, and that the only way to save your life is to practice alone without thinking of anything else. We must realize that we are standing in this fateful realm.

Everyone, think about when it rains or when a typhoon comes. Men must experience being on a boat at least once and encounter a typhoon. It sounds quite exciting when you think about it. When someone dies at sea due to a typhoon, it is pitiful, but it can be quite entertaining for children to watch. However, how nerve-wracking would that be? If you watch with a heart of pity, your heart races, but it is indeed a fascinating spectacle. When the boat rides the waves and rises to the top of the wave, you can see all the way to the bottom of the boat, but when the boat goes down with the wave, you can't even see the top of the mast. At that moment, as you worry about whether the boat will come back up, when it does rise again, you let out a sigh of relief. That is the most thrilling spectacle of all.

However, those who have experienced it and know the story well cannot enjoy it even if they are told to watch. Those who do not know can watch, but those who have experienced it cannot enjoy it. Think about it. When the boat rises to the top of a big wave and then goes down and disappears, your heart shrinks, thinking, "Has the boat capsized?" Then when the boat rises again, you exclaim, "Oh my, God is protecting it, it's rising!" That’s how it is.

When was that? It was probably around 1959 or 1960. It was before the teacher's wedding. I went fishing in the West Sea on a boat called Opal No. 8. While sitting quietly on the boat, I felt something ominous. From the moment the boat set sail, I didn't feel good. When you don't feel good, you should retreat, but I just went. I caught an octopus while fishing, but I still didn't feel good. So, I gave up on fishing and drove the boat back to shore, and sure enough, it started to rain. There were six of us, and even though we were by the beach, it was night, and I thought it wouldn't be good, so I took two people with me and left three people on the boat. The remaining three thought they were fine since they had reached the shore, saying that being there was just like being on flat ground, so they had no worries, and I left them on the boat while we came to land.

But suddenly, a typhoon began to blow. It was night, and the boat was not visible, so I thought, "They must all be dead." When dawn came and I went out, fortunately, the boat was floating on the water. However, it was rocking heavily in the waves. Being in a position of watching the people I had left behind while fishing was different. I thought it was a big deal. This old boat had been rocking all night, hanging on to a single rope, and that rope would surely snap. If that happened, the boat would drift according to the wind, right? Then it would crash into the cliffs of the big mountain on the left. What would be the next difficulty? You might think that if the boat is damaged, you can swim to the shore, but not at all. You cannot crawl out. When the water rushes in and then recedes, it is stronger than the force that pulls you by the rope, so you cannot come up to the beach and are swept back down.

Even if you reach the shore after a shipwreck, you cannot climb up if there are rocks. If it were flat ground, you could come up and live, but otherwise, you cannot. Why? Because the waves that have rushed in mercilessly wrap around and hit you. When you see people who have died, they have clawed at the ground to survive, their nails worn down and their bones protruding. They struggle to live like that.

When the waves crash against the boat, it seems like the boat and the rocks are challenging each other in strength, colliding violently, causing the boat to be shattered. But what happened to the boat then? There was a valley where the mountain range split on both sides, and the water flowed through it about five meters away, and God protected it by pushing the boat into that valley. Once it is lodged in that valley, it is hard to come out. The waves may push it further in, but it cannot come out. That is how they were saved.

So, I ran to the mountain to save those people, and the sand-like raindrops driven by the typhoon stung me sharply. It was very painful. But is there room to think about such things? Is there time to think about it? The boatman who had borrowed a day to go fishing with me was now in a life-and-death situation, and I had to run to save them, so I couldn't just stand by and watch. I had no time to think about the pain or discomfort; I forgot about myself and ran.

In that situation, I thought, "Why do I care about those people when I have no connection to them?" But I thought that God would be concerned even more than I was. I remembered the prayers I had made there. In such a situation, I realized that I could act in this way.

Then what would have been the hearts of those people? They must have been hoping that the person trying to save them would come quickly. "Oh, I'm dying, oh, I'm dying," they would have been aware of their lives hanging by a thread, feeling death thousands of times in their hearts. Because life’s joy unfolded again in such a place, new life energy emerged. Do you understand? In a place where they felt they were dying a hundred times or a thousand times, they received new salvation and resurrected, raising their hands and rejoicing. That is how it is. In a place where they did not know if they would live or die, they drew forth historical life energy, and if they filled the pit of death, they could even extend beyond that pit, giving rise to the right of resurrection.

That is why Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane before the cross, in a serious place where he did not know if he would live or die. It was not just a matter of one person dying. In such a serious place, standing beyond death and into the right of resurrection, a new historical resurrection began to unfold.

You have probably seen the act of turning a traditional Korean dress inside out. In the past, when we wore cotton pants, I saw my mother turn an old pair inside out, take out the cotton, and sew it again, making it a new pair. Similarly, that turning inside out is the right of resurrection.

Jesus said not to worry about what to eat, what to drink, or what to wear for your life, but to seek first His kingdom and His righteousness. Thus, a person who seeks righteousness becomes a resurrected person who can possess the kingdom. You must find a connection to life that is stronger than eating, drinking, or wearing. Otherwise, no matter how well you eat and dress, it is all a vain life.

You are all in a position like a boat tied at the dock. You are tied up without even realizing it. But humans live without knowing this, going back and forth. As a result, the tied rope becomes tangled. There is a rope tied, but because you do not know where it is tied, you turn this way and that, and everything gets tangled. Some people are standing sideways, some are facing the other way, and some are standing upside down, living without knowing whether there is a rope or not.

The faith path that must be hurried along
You must know that there is a lifeline. There is a lifeline. In other words, you are tied to a line connected by your bloodline.

So what must we know here? You must not be tied to that line. You must ride that line yourself. How wonderful it would be to discover that lifeline! This is the faith path that can lead you to a new life. However, having discovered this lifeline, you must not think, "What is there to hurry about? There is tomorrow and the day after; I can go anytime." You cannot think that way.

We must live our faith with the mindset that the path is long and that every moment is busy. You must know that this is the faith path, and you should always pull on that line with effort. Singing hymns and keeping time, praying and calling out to the Father, all of this is part of that effort. However, if you do it wrong, everything will go awry.

There is a saying that a mother gives milk to a crying child, right? "Father! I’m dying; you must save me!" Isn’t that God? Even if you complain like that, He saves you. (Laughter) We are doing such things. You may feel that way too. You must tie the lifeline around your waist, but without realizing it, you carry it on your back throughout your life, getting caught on stones and wobbling, causing the lifeline to break. If that string breaks, you will surely fall into hell. However, if you hold on to this lifeline, even if you fall, you will not go all the way to the bottom of hell but will get caught somewhere in the middle. That is the middle spirit world. You must understand this.

We must go along the path regardless of what others are doing, whether they are eating or resting. There are thousands of people ahead all going the same way. If you keep pulling and striving without resting, others will also wrap that line around them. In doing so, you will also feel many people falling away. It is like a marathon. As you run, there will be a first place and a second place. History is like that. For thousands of years, countless spirits have come out tied to that line. Among them, if you become first and go to that world, tying yourself to the device that wraps around, the spirit world will be restored.

To do that, we must create concrete that can wrap around it all. In other words, we must create a dock that will not let go even if the whole boat is wrapped around it. Do you understand? If such a nation is created, that nation will be the one that the Lord will come to and govern.

If South Korea is the nation where the Lord will come, it must be a nation that will not shake even if it wraps around all the nations of the world. It must be such a dock. To do that, how strong must it be? It requires cement, gravel, sand, and rebar. To make the concrete strong for the dock, we must first weave the rebar. What does rebar represent? It represents people. It means strong people among people. There must be strong people who cannot be broken or pierced. We must tie the line around those who embody such integrity and loyalty. Thus, we must have a device that can save everyone at once with just the push of a switch. That is the historical mission we have.

If the Unification Church hopes to fulfill such a tremendous mission, what will you be in making concrete? Will you be rebar, sand, or gravel? What will you be? Think about it. You should be rebar. If you cannot even be gravel, then at least be sand. If you cannot even be sand, then be water that serves others. Water can be absorbed anywhere. Everything can be tied together through the action of water. You must understand that.

Then God can save a new nation, a new country, and a new world in the future. We must create a lighthouse of life that serves as a beacon of salvation in the dark world where death waves crash. We must understand that it is our mission to create a lighthouse of life.

Following the right leader is the duty of a religious person
And the question is how strong you are and how much more you can contribute. Here, your prestige, face, and past do not matter. Once you enter the Unification Church, we all share the same fate; what difference does it make if someone is successful or not? Whether a Ph.D. enters or a former minister or a president, it is all the same. You must walk the official path you need to take.

Knowing this, what must you do here? Whether it is day or night, each person must walk their own path. If there is someone who leads you in a more righteous direction, you must simply follow that person. If he goes to the mountains, you follow him to the mountains; if he goes to the sea, you follow him to the sea; even if he goes into a swamp, you must hold onto his arm or the hem of his garment and follow him. You must establish a connection that allows you to do that. If you cannot establish that connection, it will be difficult. You must value that connection more than your own life and follow without falling away. That is the duty of religion.

That is why in Christianity, it is said that Jesus is the bridegroom and the believers are in the position of the bride. Bridegroom and bride are very good terms. They are the closest relationship. Wherever the bridegroom goes, the bride must go. The bride follows the bridegroom wherever he goes, east or west, and they must live their lives together day and night. The path they must walk is the faith path, and the relationship between the leader and the follower being referred to as bridegroom and bride is indeed a beautiful expression. Even in that, God is truly wise. Being the King of Wisdom, He has given such titles and exercised the duties of a parent to form today’s Christian cultural sphere.
You need to know that this has been done. 
That is why, for this path, one can continue on even if they die along the way without yielding. It is important to recognize that Christianity has been expanding its ties of integrity and loyalty, progressing toward an external heaven of victory until now. 
The Unification Church today is the same. The teacher himself is also on this path. He is currently heading toward that way. Even at this moment, he is going, and on this day, he is going, and throughout this month, he is going. You need to understand that this is how it is. 
From that standpoint, we must accept the hearts of the friends leading us and those who are ahead as our own, understand them, and make them our own possessions to follow. Even if it means exchanging our lives for that, even if we must die ourselves, we must hold onto his words and die, for those who are alive there will take responsibility for him and resurrect him. Do you understand what I mean? If you die while listening to his words, wouldn’t you at least receive pity? 
When you go to the spirit world, you might even pray for that person. 
Did Jesus' disciples hear Jesus' words or not? They did not, did they? If they had not heard, the relationship would be severed, and they would not be able to pray in Jesus' name. That is why, after Jesus resurrected, he asked Peter, "Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?" (John 21:15-17). This was to establish the condition that Peter had heard Jesus' words and loved him. Otherwise, considering Peter's character, he would have been the first to run away. 
Only by leaving behind the words that he died believing in Jesus, that he died listening to Jesus' words, could he receive prayers for him in the heavenly world. 
You must think that it was because of such love from God that this happened, and standing on that fateful path, you must grasp the lifeline. If you are in a position to change that line, you must change it. Thus, to go to a place of rest on the day of liberation, you must invest all your sincerity and vitality without reservation. 
In making that investment, you must become those who pledge to achieve results of value that cannot be exchanged for anything, and only then will you be equipped with the proper attitude of a faithful believer. You must understand that without this, you cannot escape the realm of death. 
<Prayer> Father, we have come to know that our connection with you is that of brothers. Since we are born as children of the same parents, we must fulfill the duty of filial piety that you desire. This filial piety should not be directed only to our earthly parents. 
If a parent rejoices only in having a filial child, it is as if they have no nation. Father, we have come to understand that when you rejoice in a filial child, you should rejoice with the nation as well. Only then can that filial child become a central being who establishes a heavenly loyalty before the nation, and thus that nation becomes the nation of the filial child, doesn’t it? 
You are, of course, seeking a filial child, and you sent Jesus to this earth as the first filial child seeking the nation of filial children. That is why he is called the only begotten son. Jesus knew that he was the only begotten son born with the love of God, representing the historical era, and he proclaimed the term "only begotten son" before the Jewish people centered on God's love. 
The only begotten son wished to be a filial child fulfilling the duty of filial piety in the bosom of the Father, but he could not just be a filial child. Even if he became a filial child, without a nation of filial children, he would inevitably be invaded by enemies. He did not realize that the heart of the Father was to love the filial child while longing for the nation of filial children. Because the hearts of the Father and the son were different, he stood in a position to pray, "Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me." 
He was in a position where he could not just be a filial child. 
Not only for myself but also in the context of the Father's heart for the nation and people, I understood that what is higher and more eternal is the nation of the Father's heart. We must understand that the reason Jesus was led to death was to establish a filial nation before the Father. 
Our own salvation is not limited to our own salvation. Please let us understand that your salvation of me is not just for me alone but for the salvation of the nation I am in. 
With my own resurrection, the nation will be resurrected, and with my own filial piety, finding the nation's filial piety is the desire of the Father. We know that to overcome the difficulties of today, we must be able to step forward to establish a nation of filial piety where the Father can dwell. We must understand that the Father is personally paving the way for us to receive such authority as sons. 
We must reflect on how many times we have treated the infinite value and deep connection you have left before us carelessly and lightly. We must repent of this fact once again. 
You have endured on the foundation of mercy and love, and we know that the thick connection of the Father's heart remains even until today through the thousands of years of historical processes that the fallen descendants of Adam have gone through. Even with just this remaining connection, we must become your sons and daughters who can feel that we cannot repay even after a thousand years of stories of repentance and gratitude. 
We have come to know that your saving me is to teach me the way to save the nation, so we must teach the descendants who follow us that this is how the nation can live, and we must also teach the brothers who are in the same situation. Only then will the parents with a filial child revive the glory of the filial child, won’t they? We, the members of the Unification Church, must become sons and daughters who can fulfill such responsibilities of a filial child today and tomorrow. 
Today, we are in an environment where waves of death are crashing from all sides. We are crying out in darkness where we cannot even know the direction, not in bright daylight, and in the moment when life bears the fate of suffering, if there is a grace that shines bright sunlight and shows us the way and direction, then those who were about to die must devote all their hearts to that grace, mustn’t they? 
Today, we have a heart of gratitude toward the Father who has shown us the bright path in His will, but we are those who have not been able to return that gratitude to the Father as it deserves with all our lives. If there are those who are saddened by the fact that they have not yet become that way, Father, please strengthen their sad hearts and guide them to repent again, I earnestly hope and wish for this. 
We must break free from this realm of fall and overcome the era of fear. When the spiritual heaven comes, it will not be a strong heaven but a fragile heaven, and we must go through a fierce battle centered around the environment of fear. We must not forget this fact. 
Without fearing such things, we must understand that this is the original path we must take and prepare ourselves to welcome the way we can go. 
If there is a leader who guides and teaches the direction we should go on this path, we must realize that we should be those who can give thanks for everything in both the heavenly and earthly worlds. Thus, we must be grateful today, grateful tomorrow, grateful this year, and grateful in the new year, striving to leave a life dedicated to gratitude. Let us know that such a group will never perish. Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this. 
Now that we know how our attitude should be, we must uphold the words of our comrades and the teachings of our teacher in pioneering our new fateful path and revolutionize and transform the environment we are in. Please let us be sons and daughters who can devote all our life force to charge toward the foundation of happiness and rest, the heavenly nest. 
Now, please take charge of the entire year following this July, which is the second half of this grace-filled year. Today is the first Sunday of the second half of this year, so bless us, and until the day this year ends, please allow us to commemorate 1970 as a year of blessings, making it the peak of our lives. 
Father, please take charge of this significant mission we are discerning today. I earnestly ask that you reveal how precious this 1970 is in the providence of restoration in history. I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
5) The Path Heaven Has Come Upon 
<Prayer> Father, we know that among the sons and daughters living on this earth, there must appear filial children who can resolve your historical grievances. 
Father, we come to understand that the reason you could endure so many hardships over the long historical process is that there was an internal power to meet the sons you longed to embrace. When we realize this, we cannot help but feel ashamed before you, wondering if we have truly become the sons and daughters you wish to meet, capable of alleviating all the difficulties of the historical process. 
We are those who, even if we dedicate our whole body and heart to become sacrificial offerings before your will, cannot fulfill any conditions to comfort you or repay you for the prolonged and sorrowful adversities you have overcome. Every time we think of our state, we feel again how pitiful you are, Father. 
We must reflect on how lonely and miserable it is for you to be in a position where you cannot boast of your beloved sons and daughters before Satan. Therefore, there must be sons and daughters on this earth whom you can trust. 
Father, we must be able to care about your dignity, honor, and circumstances. No matter how much we may seem equipped inside and out, we know that we are far too lacking and shameful to appear before your will. Therefore, we must have a humble and grateful heart before the grace you have bestowed upon us. 
Let us be your sons and daughters who understand that we must live in a position of humility, bowing our heads like servants throughout our lives and the course of our lives. 
Only by standing in such a position can we become objects of your comfort, and you can praise our humility and take pride in seeing us conform to your will. 
Father, please look upon us once again with compassion as we are not in such a position. We earnestly hope and wish that we may become sons and daughters who can bear the final cross that will remain until the end and fulfill that mission without any shortcomings. 
Among the sons and daughters gathered here this morning, if there are any whom you wish to bless, please remember them deeply in your heart and boast of them throughout the universe. There must be at least one son or daughter here who is worthy of being praised as better than anyone who has come and gone throughout the historical process. 
If we are not that way, then please personally dwell in our hearts and urge us to be strong and courageous, fulfilling our responsibilities before your will. 
Father, there will be your sons and daughters across the nation who are longing for this place, gathering their hearts to offer blessings before you. Please let your gracious hand be with them wherever they gather. 
Also, there are your children in various countries around the world who are walking the lonely path of struggle, and even at this moment, they are suppressing their lonely hearts, shedding tears, and calling upon you, so I earnestly hope and wish that you embrace them. 
Because your will, left as a bond of love, is with them, they are doing their utmost to fulfill the mission of pioneering this path. Therefore, I earnestly hope and wish that you reveal that you are with them above their heads and hearts. 
Today is the Sabbath. Please pour out your heart of compassion and love upon the places where your children gather, igniting their hearts that long for you like a flame. 
Let them become a group that wins today’s battlefield, using tomorrow’s hope as a shield, longing for you and the homeland. 
As we gather here, let each of us reflect on how much we have fulfilled the duty of loyalty and filial piety before you, and let us become children who lay down our bodies and hearts before you, committing ourselves to be stewards before the foundation you desire. 
Please be with the children of the worldwide Unification family who praise your name. Please gather and gather many of your sons and daughters to lead them toward a unified world. 
In order to reach that world quickly, please form one tribe, one nation, and one country, and further create a great nation in Asia. 
I earnestly hope and wish that a nation of blessings, a nation of love, and a nation of victory, which you delight in, will be established. 
Centered around Korea, Japan, the United States, and Germany, connecting over 40 countries, please pour out your boundless love upon the sons and daughters who are protecting the designated holy sites in those countries, so they may plant the flag of eternal victory. 
May you be with them there, so that whenever people pass by, their hearts are drawn to think of you again, creating such bonds. 
As your children have gathered here during this special period, please bless them with the ability to entrust all life’s problems to you and resolve them. 
I earnestly ask that they become sons and daughters who can receive your boundless mercy and love. 
I also earnestly ask that the remaining time be united with your will. I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
<Words> Today, many people are engaged in religious life, but not many think about the path humans take to find God or the path God takes to find humans. 
God, who cannot be met directly, 
People pray when they face difficulties, but...
I think of it as such a simple act of praying while lying down. However, the place where we pray to God is not a place where people meet and converse, but rather a place where we must understand that by praying, God establishes a relationship with us. 

The place where you live today, the place where you pray to God, does not belong to heaven. Moreover, you yourselves are not people equipped with the content that God can directly govern. When a person who is outside of direct governance prays to God in such an environment, it is not a simple matter for God to listen to that prayer and respond to fulfill it. 

There are likely many more wicked people around you than those who have set out to walk the path to heaven. This is true both personally and within families. From this perspective, we can see that families, clans, nations, and states that are on the side of evil surround us globally more than environments that would lead us to live for God. We must recognize this fact. 

This is not only the case in the flat standard of human society but also in the world beyond humans, centered on humans, in other words, the spiritual world, which is a four-dimensional world. We must understand that we are surrounded by evil spirits that cannot establish a relationship with God beyond what we feel in our daily lives. 

When we, as individuals in such an environment, pray to God, even if God wishes to listen to that prayer and respond, He cannot come directly to me from the deep, high, and holy heavenly throne. In other words, when looking at a nation, whether it is a sovereign or a president, there are various complex issues that arise when they try to connect with the most basic citizens directly. 

Therefore, when they cannot go directly, they must establish connections through sequential steps. In other words, when there is a group with an organized form, to connect from the topmost level to the lowest level, it must go through an organized order, which we can see through a nation or society. 

This is the same in the spiritual world. When you pray, you are not praying to a spirit that is directly related to you, but you are praying to the most high and holy God. However, there is a significant distance between the position of God who receives that prayer and your position. 

Thus, the question is how to fill this distance. You must understand that God, who is seated on the throne, is in a position where He must establish bridges through many people to fill this distance. Therefore, believers must go through these bridges to meet God, but until now, they have not understood this. There are many connections organized so that we can connect with our individual selves only after passing through the layered organizational society of the spiritual world. 

Thinking about this, we realize that it takes a long time for God to directly respond to our sincere prayers on earth. However, we must understand that the more sincere a person's heart is, the more the distance can be shortened. 

There is an old saying that sincerity moves heaven. This means that heaven is moved by sincerity, but simply moving heaven is not enough. We must move heaven to establish a relationship with it and bring about the results we desire. However, there is a temporal distance until the results come after heaven is moved. Yet, as such connections are made once, twice, three times, and become more frequent, we can gradually shorten the organizational form between God and ourselves. We must understand this. 

When you meet someone you do not know, you are introduced. In such cases, the person introduced establishes a relationship from the position of the person who introduced them. At that time, regardless of whether one is good or bad, the evaluation from the other party varies depending on the greatness and sincerity of the person who introduced them. 

To meet God, we must transcend all the stages between God and ourselves. Therefore, it is almost impossible for us to pave this path. The spiritual world is also surrounded by many organized environments, making it impossible for spirits to pave this path. 

The only way to pave this path is for you to put in a lot of sincerity. Thus, your sincerity must be known to God so that it can provide a motivation for God to respond. When that happens, God commands and directs. It is only through this process that a relationship is established between God and us. 

As this process is repeated once, twice, three times, and the more it increases, the more we can shorten the distance between God and humanity. In the relationship between a master and a servant, when the master dies, the servant leaves. When the master passes away, the servant packs their belongings and leaves the house. However, in a brotherly relationship, when the elder brother is in a position of dying, the younger brother will invest all his possessions and do everything possible to prevent the elder brother from dying. That is the true duty of a brother. From this perspective, Jesus and Peter could only stand in the position of a master and servant.
