6) The Significance of the Founding of the Unification Church
I praise the formation of this inter-denominational and inter-religious council. I sincerely hope that this council will serve as a new center to achieve unity and provide a strong spiritual foundation for this nation. I also sincerely thank those who established this council for including our council in the religious council in the spirit of cooperation, and I am truly grateful for your visit despite your busy schedules and the difficult circumstances around you.

I hope that this council will actively develop inter-denominational activities and become a central body that can play a new role in Korean society, leading the way in a new welfare movement.

The Motivation for Establishing the Unification Church
Now, I would like to share with the guests present how this council was established. I will briefly explain this issue. The motivation for establishing this council started from the will of God rather than the will of man.
You all know well that today's society and history are not composed solely of human relationships. There must be a greater purpose centered around faith, aiming towards a singular objective. In that sense, a society founded solely on human intentions cannot contribute to the flow of history or the new world that is to come. Thus, a new religion based on faith was established. It was thought that a religious organization could unite both human relationships and faith, and that religion must be centered on faith to bind together all that humanity desires in terms of human relationships.

So, what is faith? The intention of faith is not centered on any specific society but has a transnational, trans-denominational, and trans-national character. We can understand from history that without such a purpose, we cannot fulfill the intentions of God. In that sense, human relationships must also possess a global content that can align with the intentions of faith, rather than being based on individual or organizational desires. It is seen that the mission of religion is to integrate this understanding both internally and externally.

Then, what must exist to align faith and human relationships? There must be a content that can unite the love of God and the love of humanity. The love that allows God and humanity to become one is not centered on any specific individual, ethnic group, or nation, but must possess an emotional bond that loves humanity and the world from a transnational perspective. Therefore, the religion that seeks to find the point of convergence between faith and human relationships must not center on human relationships but must focus on how to connect human intentions to the love centered on God.

In that sense, the intentions of God and humanity must be integrated into the form of religion, with love as the central theme. This love must transcend not only specific ethnicities or nations but must be a love that surpasses all boundaries. Without this, it is impossible to form a true foundation for religion globally.

Thus far, history has been driven by sages. They have asserted their positions not only from a human perspective but also from a divine perspective. Their aims have transcended not just specific ethnicities but have crossed global boundaries. Teaching this is the role of the sages. Based on this principle, religion has emerged to connect the divine and human relationships.

Therefore, sages have established standards that bind human relationships based on the heavenly principles. However, this must be a teaching that can transcend global boundaries; this is the essence of the sages' teachings. Based on such teachings, humanity today has established moral ethics in the realm of morality.

In this context, what must the central position be for God and humanity to become one? The critical question is what the decisive center is where the love desired by God and the ideal love desired by humanity can unite. If God exists, it must be the closest position to God. The foundation that connects with God's love cannot be centered on individual love; it must be a foundation of love that can connect with the world. Without this, the love of God and the love of humanity cannot unite.

In this sense, where is the closest position where God's love and human love can connect? It is the position where human relationships follow the divine, in other words, the place where human love complies with divine love. When seeking the closest position centered on God's love, it must be the position of becoming God's true child.

If there is such a true child of God, then a true daughter of God must also be needed centered around that child. Centered on these children, there must be a true family that God can love, a true lineage that God can love, a true nation that God can love, and a true world that God can love. Thus, the Unification Church today has been founded with the question of how to establish a global standard of love between God and humanity.

God's love must be realized through historical processes, and we know well that this process has been led by the sages. Therefore, sages have been guiding humanity with the teachings of God's principles.

Now, among the sages who have come and gone throughout history, who could be the greatest sage? Of course, the teachings of their scriptures are important, but more importantly, there is a need for a religion that teaches the field where God and humanity can be closest. In this regard, considering the religions that have remained throughout history, Christianity has been introduced from a higher perspective compared to other religions, which is why the Unification Church was founded based on Christianity.

Even when looking at Jesus in Christianity, he sought a God who could be approached concretely and closely in daily life rather than an abstract God. Thus, Jesus referred to God as "my Father." There is no position higher than that of a father in a static sense. Therefore, Jesus laid the emotional foundation that could connect the relationship between God and humanity to that of father and son. This indicates that to establish a world bound by the love desired by God, there must be a static foundation.

That position must be beyond the relationship of father and son. That is why Jesus said, "God is my Father. I must be the only begotten Son who can receive God's love in the entire universe." In this light, Christianity speaks from the perspective of God's heart and presents concrete content to proclaim from the closest position to God. Moreover, Jesus also said to his followers, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." This is seen as the closest point to bind the relationship with God. He also referred to his followers as brothers, establishing the new religious ideal that all people are brothers.

The world of love that God desires must pass through such standards. The individuals whom God can love, the families composed of those individuals, the lineages formed by those families, the nations formed by those lineages, and ultimately the world that must be established through those nations must all be connected. Without such a static foundation, it cannot be realized. This must manifest in the historical process.

The purpose of God seeking humanity is that history has been guided by sages and righteous individuals. The question is how the teachings of the sages, who have represented humanity and the world, align with today's human history. If God exists, then from the beginning, God must have a direction and, through a process, create a world. If the providence of heavenly principles is behind this, we must consider how to align the historical path of humanity with that direction.

Thus, how can we restore the original relationship between God and humanity? How can we make human history centered on God's love? The question arose regarding how to align the overall content related to human history, whether it be individuals, families, specific ethnicities, or cultural backgrounds, with a worldview based on God's principles. If this second Isaac cannot fulfill their responsibility, the will of God through the three generations cannot be completed. From this perspective, we can see that the responsibility of King David was more important than that of the other kings centered around King Saul and King Solomon.

Thus, considering various historical facts, we can understand that the position of the second is a crucial position that can determine the resolution of the ultimate mission.

The rise and fall are determined centered on the second. 
So why is the second position problematic? The will must pass through three stages to be fulfilled. From God's perspective, if we consider God as the first stage, Adam and Eve correspond to the second stage. In other words, if God is the first stage, then Adam and Eve are the second stage.

Just as the duality of God's masculine and feminine aspects must become one, Adam and Eve, who were separated as male and female, must also become completely united. Only then can they become one with God again.

What can bind this together is God's love and the love of humanity, the love of Adam and Eve. It remains as something that has not been connected.

The form that combines Adam and Eve again is the children. In this way, the first, second, and third generations are formed centered on God.
Then, among these three generations, the problem arose in which generation? It was in the second generation, the generation of Adam and Eve. Adam and Eve could not become one centered on God's love. God created Adam as the representative of the plus character centered on the individuality of the being and loved that son the most. In loving that son, He combined feminine love. In loving Eve, the daughter, He also combined masculine love.
By the two that have been separated becoming one, the origin of the third beginning emerges. <Words> Humans always think centered around themselves. They also think centered around their families and their countries. Thus, people always think centered around themselves or their surroundings, which you may have felt in your daily lives. 

However, when we consider the position we stand in or the position of the country we live in, we can see that individuals or nations cannot be the center. Even when looking at families, we know well that if a family is a good family, it cannot stand as a central family representing good families. 

From this perspective, when we think about the relationship between the will and ourselves, we can understand that we should not center ourselves when walking the path of the will. The will is a process that moves forward through the past, present, and future centered on an unchanging single purpose, and within that, various circumstances unfold. Just as there are spring, summer, autumn, and winter in a year, and all 365 days are different, the providential will also sends forth years and days toward a single purpose, and those years and days are not all the same. 

In such a situation, the country that stands there thinks based on its position, and you change your thoughts according to the circumstances. We often talk about public positions and private positions. A public position is one that opposes one's own position, while a private position is one that opposes the public position. It is difficult for a person to stand in a public position. From the moment one wakes up, it is easy to live the entire day from a self-centered perspective, and it is also easy to live one's life that way. This is the lifestyle habit of people living on this earth. 

Then, how should we move away from this private position to establish a relationship with the public position? We must overcome all private conditions and transcend all private environments, and we must renew and reorganize the self we are currently in. Without doing so, we know well from our daily lives that it is difficult to establish a relationship with the public position. 

When we look at the duty of loyalty to the nation, the loyal subject and I are far apart, and when we consider the duty of filial piety to our parents at home, that filial piety and I are also distant. Just like the duty of filial piety at home and the duty of loyalty centered on the nation, when we consider the duties of saints centered on the world, you are in a distant position. 

This is because the will does not represent individuals or families, nor does it represent nations or the world. Therefore, we can infer that in order to get closer to the will, the conditions we must overcome will also increase in proportion to that distance. 

Thus, if people walking the path of the will think that they will always walk a smooth and happy path that the world will see as good, that is a great illusion. The more one stands in a public position, the less one can stand in a private position, and therefore unimaginable difficulties will arise before that path. It is reflected and manifested in a position that cannot be compared to the individual. You will understand this well if you sincerely wish to walk the path of the will. 

The reason why conditions of indemnity are necessary 
For us living on this earth, bad things must come before good things. Also, after experiencing bad things, good things must come. Just as there is a peak and a valley on a mountain, the peak and the valley are absolute factors in forming the mountain. If they are not far apart and there is no gap, a high mountain cannot be formed. In other words, the peak and the valley have a relative relationship, and at the same time, they have a homogeneous position that forms one mountain. 

So do people prefer the valley or the peak? Everyone prefers the peak over the valley. However, one can only ascend to the peak by going through the valley. The deeper one feels the valley, the more one feels the value of sincerity. 

Similarly, in the path of life, those who wish to walk the high road must have the central qualifications to conquer the entire valley. Without that, we must understand that we cannot occupy the summit. 

Now, when we think about the will and ourselves, the Unification Church and the will, the Unification Church and this country, the Unification Church and Asia, the Unification Church and the world, and the Unification Church and the issues of heaven and earth, it is easy to say, but where exactly is the path that the Unification Church must take? When we look at this issue, the Unification Church is neither situated in the valley nor at the summit. Our reality is that we are not established anywhere, so we must surely establish a foundation. 

If such a foundation is not established, then one person must take responsibility for it. That is a more difficult path than ascending to the summit or descending into the valley. Therefore, we must establish conditions that can allow everything to remain. Without that, you must understand that it is impossible to stand in a normal position. This is why conditions of indemnity are necessary. 

What are conditions of indemnity? Since no one can bear that task itself, one stands in a position where they have fulfilled it by having an overall form as a condition. In other words, it is about creating a model of a high mountain and taking on the intermediate responsibility of carrying out or embracing what could not be fulfilled from the mid-point between the high peak and the deep valley. You must understand that such conditional indemnity is necessary. 

From the perspective of the will, the second time is always a problem 
When I think about the past that I have walked until now, whenever I wanted to decide on something I liked, I never requested it from God from a human standpoint. Such requests should not be made. That is something I always worry about. I have thought about whether I have put more sincerity into it than God and whether I have become more concerned about the path of the will than God. If I do not do that and do not align completely with God, I know that there will definitely be indemnity. 

Throughout my journey on the path of the will, I had friends. However, now when I quietly think about those friends, I realize that God has taken away all the friends who were close to me. I wondered why that happened, and I realized it was because I easily forget the position of having to bring God due to them. This is the flaw of humanity. 

On this earth, it is difficult to break away from habitual living environments and difficult to escape from the connections of circumstances. This is the flaw of humanity. Therefore, in emotional issues, human loyalty issues, or business issues, if one decides without relying on God from a human perspective or if there is a concern that such matters may be more important than God, God has separated such environments from me. I always feel this. However, there is also the opposite side. 

Indemnity must occur either from the highest position or from the lowest position. Indemnity from the highest position is a condition of indemnity from a public position centered on God, but indemnity from the lowest position is something that God establishes as a new and good foundation. You can feel this well in your daily life. Last year, we transitioned into the 1970s in this way. 

Looking at it from the perspective of the will until now, the second time has always been a problem. The second son has always been a problem. In the family of Adam, the second son Abel was a problem, in the family of Noah, the second son Ham was a problem, and in the family of Abraham, the second son Isaac was a problem. Furthermore, throughout the 6,000 years of history, Jesus, who came as the second Adam, was a problem. 

Thus, the second person, or the second family, or the country that took on the second responsibility has always been a problem. 

Looking at the 6,000 years of history from the perspective of the will, the first Israel was the Jewish nation, the second Israel was the Christian realm, and the third Israel can be said to be today's Korea. However, if we look at it centered on the nation, the first Israel was a nation where God could be with the land, but the second Israel formed only a spiritual national authority and has pursued that nation for the past 2,000 years. Thus, this era is a global issue centered on Korea.

Because the Unification Church is active for the nation, the nation will create an external environment that can develop the Unification Church.

Look at the people who come out of our victorious training sessions. How can they change so much? How can they change so much after just four days of training? Recently, when we gathered 270 local leaders for training, they initially fought among themselves and various issues arose, but after five days of training, they were amazed at how much they had changed, and they themselves were curious about it. There is certainly something they do not understand. No matter how much we ask, they do not know why it is so. It seems trivial, yet it is extraordinary.

During this training period, the head of the information department of the police station responsible for ideological issues came in for training, with a special order from the police chief that they must be trained first. In the future, all police chiefs will receive training.

At first, they came saying things like, “What is the Unification Church?” and felt embarrassed, and some elders from established churches were skeptical, but by the time they finished training and were about to leave, they bowed their heads. At that time, they would complain, asking why we treated them as enemies. Did we ask them for food or clothing? Did we demand that they give up their living rooms? What did we do? Even so, do we have many people who we took from established churches? A few people came to become new people, but it is unreasonable to treat us like enemies for the sake of those few.

They know that they will be absorbed by us. If they know that, would they remain silent? If that is the case, they should let it be. However, without knowing that, they criticize the church, saying this and that about the Unification Church, while the teacher, Moon, is still living in the shadows but is preparing everything.

Even looking at the recent WACL (World Anti-Communist League) National Conference held in Japan, it is evident. From the Prime Minister to the Deputy President of the Liberal Democratic Party, and various figures like Secretary General Roski and former Prime Minister Kishi, they have recently been featured in newspapers discussing the WACL conference, which is astonishing. Why are they doing that? I see through it. Such things are being done by Koreans now.

That is why do not think of the Unification Church as a church for Teacher Moon. I do not want to have the consciousness of being Teacher Moon of the Unification Church. I just think of myself as one of the Unification Church members. If not, nothing will be accomplished. That is the teacher’s philosophy of life.

Walk the public path
No matter how tired I am, when I am tired, I engage in exercise to relieve that fatigue. While ordinary people just want to rest, I cannot allow myself that. I can relieve fatigue through exercise as much as I want.

Living a public life is difficult. You should think about this and consider the relationship between purpose and us, purpose and the nation. Can a person who lives centered on themselves work for the world? They cannot. Can a person who lives centered on themselves become the center of the nation or the center of the family, or work for their neighbors? A person who is centered only on themselves cannot prevent their own body from doing what it wants. Gathering money to the point where one cannot even attend church on Sundays, while claiming to understand life, is not the path that conscience desires. The path we must take is not a private path but a public one.

A person who wants to walk the public path must shed public tears, public blood, and public sweat. Nothing can be accomplished with blood and sweat shed for personal reasons. If one sheds blood and sweat for personal reasons, it becomes a motivation for failure, leading to quicker ruin. Tears shed for oneself and blood and sweat shed for oneself, no matter how much, will not remain for future generations.

However, public work is fundamentally done for others. Doing for others ultimately means doing for the nation. The nation is larger than one’s own home and broader than one’s own relatives. Therefore, the path of a loyal subject is to go even if it means abandoning one’s parents, and the path of a loyal subject is to go even if it means abandoning one’s beloved spouse. A person who prioritizes their own desires and only focuses on their own kin cannot become a loyal subject.

The path of a saint is to disregard the nation and go for the world. Therefore, as citizens of the Republic of Korea, we should not only go for the Republic of Korea but also go for the world, even if it means the nation will perish. That is the path of a saint. Today, the members of the Unification Church must walk the path that saints have not yet walked. That is our path. Therefore, you must learn to go out for more public matters.

In this perspective, do not feel sad about the issue of the association president. The issue is how much you can unite with the purpose through this event. Through this event, you should be able to say that you will complete the great task of national restoration that he left behind, which he could not accomplish on this earth. Also, we must unite in our hearts to fulfill the increased responsibilities we have as Unification Church members who must pray for the world. This is a more important issue. I hope you will spend this time solemnly thinking about such things. Do you understand? “Yes.”

Now, stop wiping the tears you have been shedding and do not shed tears within the Unification Church. The general public who have been saying this and that about the Unification Church must have all said that the Unification Church will collapse now that the association president has died. However, no matter how much they say that, we will never perish. If they want to promote it, let them. The more they do, the more they will be consumed by it. We are confident that we will not perish. We are confident. When you have confidence, things will turn out as they should.

The teacher has gone through all sorts of experiences, but God has protected him. When spring comes, snakes shed their skins, right? To shed their skin, they need something opposing, that is, the cracks in the rocks. It is the same. That is how I think. Therefore, especially during such times, you must think about how you can share the burden with God.

Those who oppose the Unification Church and have stood on the opposing side will find it difficult to return in the future. God will continue to take away famous people and politicians from around the world as needed.

The teacher has shed blood and sweat for the Republic of Korea until now. I have been loyal to this nation and this people. However, I have been turned away, insulted, and laughed at by this nation and this people. In such situations, it is useless to make excuses, but the teacher did not make excuses either.

Silence was the only thing that had to be accepted publicly. That is why we were able to lay a global foundation.

Forgiveness also follows heavenly principles
Now, even if you say not to reveal it to the world, it will inevitably be revealed. Therefore, the day will come when the Unification Church will lead the Republic of Korea. If not, then the God I have served until now is wrong. However, this does not come from mere greed. It is the result of the teacher sleeping less, eating less, playing less, and shedding tears of blood. That path is never a path to ruin. You must understand that. I have fought and come this far while being imprisoned for the sake of that one day.

Regardless of any church or denomination, when the teacher rises to the top, they will have no choice but to meet him in a position where they bow their heads. The teacher can curse just as well as anyone else, and he can analyze human psychology to a degree that no one else can match. So, do not think even a little bit anxiously. The association president has gone, but do not worry about earthly matters. Understand the teacher’s intention to comfort you, and each of you should take on the responsibilities of the association president. Do you understand? “Yes.” Therefore, you must pray for his soul until the 28th, saying that you will fulfill what he left undone. You must be able to say that you will take responsibility for what he could not accomplish. 

How much has the former association president suffered in the past? There have been countless such incidents. Each time, he directly or indirectly helped the teacher and handled all matters.
It has been. The president who has gone to the spirit world is not the problem. Understanding this, I ask you to become the sons and daughters of unity who will not lack in walking the public path. Do you understand? "Yes."

10) The Limits of Life and Death

I believe that younger people have also thought about how they will live their lives and meet their end in various ways. 

God desires the tragedy of humanity to be resolved.
Of course, one thing we must understand for generations to come is that the affairs of the earth and the affairs of heaven do not proceed in parallel. The work of humans on earth and the work of God are always concealed and developed in opposing environments. This is the tragedy of God and the tragedy of humanity.

If the path centered around human ethics aligns with a principle and is in harmony with divine principles, then all the joys that occur in the human world today will become God's joy, and all the sorrows that occur in the human world will become God's sorrow.

If God is omnipotent, can He give joy and sorrow to humanity at the same time? God must have placed joy above and sorrow as a reaction. Just as there is a shadow where there is substance, and just as there is a valley where there is a high mountain. It may be necessary to have sorrow as a stimulating factor in a relative relationship, but if sorrow was given to diminish joy, we can conclude that God cannot be the omnipotent God.

If anyone were to ask about the history of humanity up to today, they would not hesitate to say that human life is a tragedy and that the history through which humanity has lived is itself a tragedy. No matter whom you ask, we are living in such an era, and our ancestors also lived through such a historical period.

Then, if such a history has been woven from the past to the present, what will tomorrow be like in this moment heading toward a new historical era, enveloped by the environment of the times? Is it God's desire to pass on all the sorrows that have existed from the past to tomorrow as sorrows? If there is someone on earth with a certain purpose, they too would not want to pass on that sorrow to future generations; they would want to end it in their own generation. This applies universally, whether globally, nationally, collectively, or within families, and the limits of this are diverse. Even with such limits, a person with a conscience thinks they want to leave a legacy of goodness within those limits. This is our natural mindset inherited from our innate connections.

When we see it this way, what we need to consider today is whether there is a way to stop this tragic history and all factors of sorrow in my generation. If it cannot be done in my generation, can it be done centered around our family? If it cannot be done through family, can it be done through relatives, clans, or tribes? If that does not work, can it be done through any other ethnicity? If it cannot be done through ethnicity, can it be done by establishing a sovereign nation? This is a significant matter for those who wish to leave a good future and a joyful and happy future.

God would not have thought of allowing this history of sorrow to continue into the future, either in the past or in the present. Therefore, if there is someone who can take on such a tragedy, God would not hesitate to say, "Ah, the reality of the desire I wanted to leave behind has appeared!" and would want to welcome history. If such a family were to appear, God would want to entrust all the sorrows of the world to that family and place everything before them. Furthermore, if there is a clan that can do so, He would want to entrust it to that clan. Wouldn't this be God's heart?

If there is a nation that does not wish for the foundation of such resentment to remain in the future and asks to take on the responsibility of preventing such disasters, God would not hesitate to entrust the entire history woven with sorrow to that nation. Even if it means sacrificing one nation or one country, God would want to immediately place that sorrow and difficulty before them. No matter how sorrowful and terrible the situation of that nation may be, you must think that there is a heart of the Father who wants to overcome and transcend it.

Then, what is the reason God chose the chosen people in such a historical era? The reason God established the chosen people of Israel was to ultimately enjoy global happiness and to take on the sorrows of history. God did not establish them to enjoy historical happiness. You must clearly understand that the chosen people of Israel were not established to be happy and joyful only for themselves, trapped in the highest sense of authority, with their own independent sovereignty.

From this perspective, what is the reason for establishing religion? We must find a true form that can do so, but because that cannot be found all at once, we have been tracing the backgrounds of numerous tribes throughout history to cultivate a single form. In order to prepare a foundation for the restoration, God has nurtured many religions to discern the sincerity of each nation.

Then, religious individuals must have faith and sincerity, hoping for the emergence of a person, a tribe, a nation, or a state that can take on the historical sorrows.

So, where has such a responsible religion been? To my knowledge, there has not been such a religion until now. Even Judaism in Israel could not do so. That is why God sent Jesus Christ, His Son, to this earth to elevate Judaism to a new level and to pass it on to individuals. We must understand that this Son came to show the way to prepare a foundation of happiness for all people, overcoming the sorrows of humanity and the historical path.

Jesus came to this earth with such a purpose, but He could not establish that will and ended up being crucified. Among the countless saints who believed in that will, many voluntarily sought the path of death to regain their personal salvation, but were there any martyrs in the historical era who had the desire to leave behind a single precious child who could take on the sorrows of history and the sorrows of the future? There were none.

When we look at this, the history of Christianity has been a history of martyrdom, shedding blood until now, and has gone through the path of suffering. However, if there is not a single person who can do so in the end times of history, where could there be anyone more pitiful than God? You must understand this clearly.

God has gathered many religions and has now left behind the forms of four major religions. What God desires is to entrust to Christianity, which has been pushed to the limits of the last days, not only the historical sorrows but also the sorrows of the times and the sorrows that will come in the future. To do this, He must welcome a Son who can take on the sorrows of history on behalf of God, take responsibility for the entire world, the entire universe, and all of humanity, and say that He will indemnify this history of sorrow. However, when we see Christianity, which is not even prepared to welcome such a Son, we must feel that God is indeed a pitiful being.

At this moment, I reflected once again on the vow I made before God long ago. God has sought a Son who can take on this mission, which no one knows in the course of history. So, who will that Son be? Is it someone named Moon from the Unification Church who has come out to take on that responsibility? I actually came out for that purpose. I have thought that way and have awaited the day when it can be done.

However, in the process of walking that path, the responsibility our association must take is to satisfy the sorrows that God bears and to take on the world. In order to fulfill such a responsibility as a Son, a relative environment must be prepared. Only then can we determine a complete limit that can be responsible as individuals and establish a standard of life before the realm of death. However, seeing that such a limit has not yet been determined, it indicates that there are still sacrificial conditions for indemnification remaining in the relative environment.

Therefore, as I carry out my purpose today, whether it is through family or organization, or if a Son goes to such a position, I cannot be sad. I must not be sad. What God intends to establish through me is not to leave behind a history of sorrow but to leave behind a history of joy. Therefore, whenever I face such problems, I must cry out toward a new world beyond this harsh environment and resolve to take full responsibility for all the sad contents of tomorrow's history.

Long ago, I prayed before the Father about where the leader of our association should go. I held hands with my mother and prayed tears of supplication. What I desire is neither to live nor to die. It is simply that the will of the Father must not die, and the mission of the Father must not die. Therefore, even if we die, the will of the Father must live, and even if we are sacrificed, the will of the Father must remain. When I think of this, I realize that if there is a way to preserve the will, even if the Son dies a million times, I must send that path of death with joy, understanding the heart of God.

So, when I heard the news that such things had happened, I felt, "The time has come!" and I realized that God is truly a sorrowful being. I know better than anyone the internal and external struggles that the Son faced in the 1960s, trying to devote himself to the will despite his disability.

While in prison, I had an unforgettable shocking impression. Therefore, I wanted to ensure that even if I had to pay any price of sacrifice in my lifetime, I would like to relieve him of his disabled state. My heart was that if he could have a healthy body for even one day, as a son of God, and smile with a joyful face while serving God, it would be worth it. That is why I ordered him to undergo surgery. I felt that it was time for him to shed blood when considering all the paths that the will had taken.

When I see that he was hospitalized under the command of the Teacher and went according to the Teacher's will, my hope is that even if the whole association cannot take on the path of suffering today, I wish that a Son would take responsibility for at least a part of the sorrow. I feel that I cannot earnestly pray for his recovery and have entrusted it to God. Why? Because the time is approaching when we must not leave the sorrows of the world behind in order to take on this vast world. This is certain.

The principle of indemnity does not allow for forgiveness. Today, the time of suffering that must be taken on personally, as a family, as an organization, nationally, in Asia, and globally is approaching. The question is how to prevent this.

However, you must understand that there is no forgiveness in the principle of indemnity. There has been no forgiveness for me either. In my more than 50 years of life, I have lost all the friends I loved. I have lost all the younger siblings I cherished.

When I think of this, I reflect on whether I have stood in a position where I loved them more than God during this period. I worry that because I loved the leader of the association before God loved him, that love may have become a burden to God. Beyond that, since I have already entrusted his departure to God, I have tried to let go of any lingering attachments.

Now, what you must understand is where the limit of life and death is determined. Who will resolve the resentment of the fallen historical era, and which nation or country will resolve it? Without resolving this issue, we cannot establish a realm of life in the realm of death.

From this perspective, among the blessed families today, there may have been families that worried about their own families in the 1960s and 1970s, but simply worrying about their own families will not easily resolve the path of suffering for that family. Blessed families must think about their nations and the world beyond their own families. Why is that? Because God's providence of restoration is seeking individuals, families, tribes, and nations that can indemnify this sorrowful history. That is why God established the nation of Israel, but when they could not take responsibility and lost it, He established Christianity, and when that also failed, He is drawing a boundary for the life rights of the third Israel.

What kind of organization can take on such responsibilities before God? It is neither today's Christianity nor Buddhism. It is none of the religious organizations on this earth. No matter how you look at it, it must be our Unification Church.

What God is seeking is to gather families that can indemnify the global sorrows of history and resolve the sorrows of the suffering history, organize tribes, and organize nations from those tribes, forming a nation that can fulfill the priestly mission of preventing global disasters. Who will create a nation that can take on such responsibilities? You must understand that it is only our Unification Church.

Until we walk this path, even if we have money, it is still a cross. If we do not have sons and daughters who can go for that purpose and that meaning, it will be a burden. In other words, if we do not have such sons and daughters standing before that purpose, we will become a burden, and if blessed families do not have such sons and daughters, they must take on that responsibility. Let us not mourn for children who are sacrificed for the purpose. Today, the members of the Unification Church have followed the teacher until now.
